Current Affairs Commentary

World Animal Day

— Du

Today is World Animal Day. All European and American countries have grand commemorations and extensive public opinion campaigns for this day. Famous people give public speeches, and radio broadcasts are used to explain the significance of animal protection. Some schools have mandatory lessons to raise awareness among students. As for personal expressions, they are too numerous to count. The Animal Protection Society of this city has also decided to hold a public awareness meeting on this day to align with the world, embody Heaven's virtue of loving life, and strive to eliminate cruelty and killing. The intentions of benevolent gentlemen are worthy of praise.

The animal protection movement began long ago, more than a century ago. At that time, animal cruelty was prevalent in England. Under the protection of the Church, animal protection societies were organized. However, the roots were not firm, and the response was minimal. It was not until 1835, with the strong support of Queen Victoria and the passage of laws in Parliament to protect all livestock, that the society was able to celebrate a smooth future and establish a permanent foundation. Today, animal protection is a familiar term, and the atmosphere has long permeated the world. Germany, France, the United States, Italy, Austria, Belgium, Czechoslovakia, Denmark, Finland, the Netherlands, and other countries all have animal protection organizations. The Animal Protection Society of our country was also established in Shanghai last February, following in their footsteps and contributing to the cause. The achievements of the past year are already evident. For example, establishing release gardens, hiring veterinarians, relocating aquatic animals from the Yuyuan Temple Nine-Bend Bridge, requesting the Zhejiang Provincial Government to stop the capture and killing of stray dogs in various counties, and contributing suggestions to the Public Works Department to strengthen the prohibition of animal cruelty. All of these are targeted at addressing urgent needs based on facts. Are we not willing to extend our deepest sympathy to this compassion for all creatures, not just paying lip service?

Some may think that the world is filled with murderous intent, the prelude to a great war is about to begin, and humanity has no time to protect livestock when it is busy slaughtering each other. Moreover, even in terms of unethical treatment, the suffering of humans is probably far greater than that of livestock. How can we devise a comprehensive plan to prevent such inhumane and cruel acts from recurring in today's world? However, animal protection is something that ordinary people can easily influence and directly address. Preventing cruelty and killing cannot be achieved by simple actions. We can only focus on what is close and easy to do, hoping to use the power of continuous publicity to slightly reduce the signs of gratuitous cruelty, and further want to base this concept of animal protection to gradually promote a sense of mutual compassion among humans, so that they can gradually transform each other, think of love and help, and thereby automatically stop their cruel acts and abandon the evil thoughts of war. Therefore, the significance of animal protection today, when extended, is certainly sufficient to achieve the ultimate goal of safeguarding humanity.

Dike Breach on the Xiaoyi River in Haizhou; Salt River Under Pressure, Rising Water Threatens Xinpu; Part of Guanyun Affected by Disaster; Jiaomu Transportation Cut Off

(Xuzhou) Donghai Telegraph, The Yellow River water downstream of Liutang surged violently, and the Xiaoyi River dike in Donghai suddenly breached several tens of meters yesterday. The water flowed south, affecting part of Guanyun County. In addition, the Salt River was also under pressure and flooded, threatening Xinpu. People from all walks of life are inspecting the water situation and are rushing to build ten embankments day and night. The Huangfang Associations of Donghai and Shuyu counties re-telegraphed Guanyun, requesting that the Chaimi Salt River gate and dam be opened quickly to release water into the sea. (Special Telegram, 3rd)

(Qingjiangpu) Pingshang, Tanggou, Datongxingyao, and Liheng townships in the Fifth District of Shuyang, were flooded because of the breach of the Pingdun embankment on the left bank of the Chaimi River. In addition, the area east of Wuji in the Fifth District is a vast expanse of water. Transportation between Haizhou and Shuyu has been cut off. The Datang embankment, which protects Pingshang Tangshui, also breached yesterday, and the water flowed directly to the Zhoujia River mouth. The district office has chosen a place to relocate. (Special Telegram, 3rd)

(Qingjiangpu) Within the Huai-Pi section of the second section of the Flood Prevention, the Yun embankment at Qilijiafang north of Zaohe overflowed, with a length of about 40 meters. The Telegraph Office reported the progress of the emergency repairs on the 2nd. (Special Telegram, 3rd)

(Qingjiangpu) According to the Flood Prevention Office, the Weishui water level stabilized today. Yaowan rose one inch, with a current level of 275 inches. Suqian rose two inches, with a current level of 224 inches. Qingjiang rose two inches, with a current level of 252 inches. (Special Telegram, 3rd)

(Nanjing) The flood disaster in northern Jiangsu is becoming increasingly severe, and various counties have requested the Huai River Diversion Association to remove the water-gathering dams. Xu Kai issued a statement on the 2nd, stating that the construction of the Liulaojian water-gathering dam on the Central Canal was based on the decision of the Economic Committee and the Huangfang Association, which was to divert the Huang River water south into Weishan Lake and then into the sea through the Central Canal and the Liutang River. Recently, detailed measurements showed that the flow rate through Liutang was approximately 800 cubic meters per second, while the flow rate through the Liulaojian water-gathering dam into the canal downstream was also 500 cubic meters. The water level difference between the upstream and downstream of the water-gathering dam was about 18 centimeters, which had very little impact on the flow of the Central Canal in Liutang. He and the Jiangsu Provincial Government are currently requesting instructions from the Economic Committee on how to handle this. However, after careful study, it was found that the Liutang Central Canal is currently the only way to discharge the Yellow River water. The Yellow River mouth has not been blocked, and the accumulated water is too high, and the inflow is surging, far exceeding the drainage capacity, causing the water level to rise daily and expanding the disaster area. In reality, the water-gathering dam has no significant impact. (Central News Agency Telegram, 3rd)

Yellow River Water Continues to Rise in Sui Territory

(Tianjin) Suidian Tuoke County Telegraph, According to the report from the head of the First District, the Yellow River has risen by more than two feet in the past five days, and the Heihe River has risen by about one foot. It is still rising. In addition to supervising strict blockages, a telegram is respectfully reported. Sazhou County Telegraph, The Yellow River water rose another inch today, but there is no danger. The 27th Yellow River water rose another two inches, and the situation is still dangerous. In addition, Feng Heming, the head of the surveying team of the Suiyuan Provincial Government, telegraphed the province, The river water is rising rapidly, and both banks have overflowed, flooding many fields. The water situation in the west of the river is particularly severe, with a flooded area of more than ten li. Surveying work is difficult. (Special Telegram, 3rd)

Xubu Shelters Refugees; All Repatriated Out of the Territory

(Xuzhou) Xubu sheltered more than 2,000 refugees. Because there were no funds to support them, they were all repatriated on the 2nd. Trains were provided on the Tianjin-Pukou and Longhai Railways to transport them home. They spent the night at the station platform, crying and shouting, making a terrible scene. They were all transported away on the morning of the 3rd. (Special Telegram, 3rd)

Thirteen-Nation Committee Meeting Discusses Sanctions Issue; Research Steps to be Decided by the Executive Yuan; Britain Plans Vigorous and Swift End to the War; France Still Does Not Abandon Conciliatory Action

(Geneva) The League of Nations Executive Council's Thirteen-Nation Committee is scheduled to meet at 4:00 PM. The chairman is Spanish representative Madariaga. The discussion will focus on the issue of sanctions. Since the war in East Africa has already begun, the question is whether the League of Nations will immediately implement sanctions under Article 16 of the Covenant or follow the original procedure of the Thirteen-Nation Committee drafting a report and recommendations based on Article 15 of the Covenant. This will be considered. Therefore, the Thirteen-Nation Committee must discuss whether the Italian army's invasion of Abyssinia constitutes an "unprovoked aggression" and whether Article 16 of the Covenant can be invoked to declare sanctions. Once the Executive Yuan holds its meeting on Saturday, the task of the Thirteen-Nation Committee will come to an end. The Executive Yuan will then decide on the steps to be taken. Regarding the Abyssinian Emperor's request to send an investigation team, experts from Britain, France, and Spain will submit a report to the Thirteen-Nation Committee, stating that since war has already broken out on the Abyssinian border, sending an investigation team would be futile and dangerous. (Havas dispatch on the 3rd)

(Geneva) After the telegram from the Abyssinian Emperor to the League of Nations accusing Italy of invading the Abyssinian border was received, it was distributed to all members of the League of Nations Executive Council. The Executive Council is likely to convene a meeting in Geneva. The Executive Council can be convened at any time today. Except that today's Thirteen-Nation Committee is convening, the Abyssinian administration is in complete disarray. The Italian delegation is almost entirely in Rome, with only a few low-ranking officials remaining in Geneva. Various parties related to the League of Nations currently do not believe that Mussolini has made a final decision. The news of Italian troops violating the border reported from Abyssinia and the total mobilization test conducted in Rome yesterday have caused great shock here. However, the Italian side believes that the actions of the Italian army do not indicate that the war has begun, but merely a movement towards strategic positions. The Executive Council may immediately decide to arrange aerial surveillance to determine whether Italian troops have invaded Abyssinian territory in the northeast corner of Wossa province, near Mount Moussa Ali. If there is indeed a border violation, the Executive Council will convene a meeting, and the League of Nations General Assembly may also be reconvened. According to independent sources in Geneva, approximately 50,000 Italian troops with aircraft are concentrated near Mount Moussa Ali. The border line in that area is slightly ambiguous, so it cannot be determined with certainty at this time whether Italian troops have actually entered Abyssinian territory. Today, when the Thirteen-Nation Committee convenes, it will discuss the Abyssinian Emperor's suggestion to send League of Nations observers to conduct on-site inspections. At the same time, Mussolini's speech in Rome yesterday is seen here as having left very little hope for peace. Many observers believe that this is the final declaration before taking action. One commentator even called it a "war speech." (Reuters dispatch on the 3rd)

(London) Britain's opposition to Italy's use of force is becoming increasingly strong today. Those close to Prime Minister Baldwin say that the Prime Minister will respond to Italian Prime Minister Mussolini's speech when he speaks at the Conservative Party conference in Bournemouth on Thursday. It is also said here that Mussolini's speech has made the British Cabinet determined to curb his ambitions and to swiftly end this dispute through collective sanctions. (National Telegraph on the 2nd)

(London) Britain is prepared to fulfill its promise to impose sanctions on Italy, but only on the condition of cooperation from other countries. Before today's Cabinet meeting, Foreign Secretary Hoare and War Secretary Hore-Belisha met with the King. After the meeting, the War Secretary, the First Lord of the Admiralty Monsell, and the Secretary of State for Air Londonderry held another meeting, which shows that Britain has already implemented its announced policy. It is reported that the Cabinet discussed whether to inquire with Germany and the United States about their attitude towards League of Nations sanctions against Italy. The questions for inquiry will include the following three points: (1) Instructing Minister Eden to solemnly declare at the League of Nations that Britain will not act alone; (2) If Italy is indeed the aggressor, then the arms embargo can be lifted; (3) British-French cooperation to deal with the European crisis. (National Telegraph on the 2nd)

(Paris) The British and French representatives attending the League of Nations meeting have exchanged views on the issue of imposing sanctions on Italy and have reached a consensus. It is believed that a gradual approach should be adopted, and it is believed that these sanctions will be limited to economic measures, such as refusing loans to Italy and prohibiting the export of raw materials to Italy. In addition, the French Foreign Ministry has stated to the British government that France does not intend to impose sanctions unless it is a collective action. Therefore, the attitude of officials is more optimistic than before, believing that it will not be long before drastic sanctions are implemented. It is also believed that the tense international situation will not increase at present, and it can be seen from the attitudes of Britain and Italy that the danger in the Mediterranean is still expected to decrease. As for the British government's previous inquiry to France regarding whether the French Navy will cooperate with the British Navy if the British fleet in the Mediterranean is attacked, France's reply will not be decided until the Cabinet meeting on Friday. (Havas dispatch on the 3rd)

(London) It is reported that the British Cabinet meeting decided to instruct Minister Without Portfolio Eden that if news of war between Italy and Abyssinia is confirmed, he should request the League of Nations General Assembly and Executive Council to convene meetings immediately. However, in any case, there will be no such action before Friday, as Eden must wait until tomorrow to leave London and will not arrive in Geneva until October 4th. Also, Eden will meet with French Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval en route to Geneva. Regarding the British inquiry about what attitude France would take if the British Mediterranean fleet were attacked, a reply from France should be available soon. In addition, the first thing Britain should do is lift the arms embargo on Abyssinia. The Cabinet has decided to do so immediately after Italy and Abyssinia officially declare war. Officials believe that sanctions can only be limited to economic measures, while business and industry figures still oppose cutting off trade relations with Italy, saying that it would harm the interests of many countries. If it is unavoidable, then it must be done gradually. (Havas dispatch on the 3rd)

(Paris) France has informally indicated to Britain that the French government will give an affirmative answer to the British government's request for joint British and French naval action in the Mediterranean. (National Telegraph on the 3rd)

(Paris) According to French sources, Italian Ambassador to France Cerruti visited French Prime Minister Laval yesterday and reiterated that if Britain only implements economic and financial sanctions against Italy, the Italian Navy will definitely not launch an attack in the Mediterranean against the British fleet. The opinion in Paris is that since the British government has stated that it does not want to take any action unless it is a collective one, France is now not giving up "conciliatory action." Informed sources here believe that any sanctions will not be excessive and will not cause international tension, so the European dispute in the Mediterranean seems to be avoidable. (Reuters dispatch on the 3rd)

(Paris) After French Prime Minister Laval attends the Cabinet meeting on Friday, British Minister Without Portfolio Eden will bring instructions to Paris to assist the French Prime Minister in formulating the "guidelines" for the Thirteen-Nation Committee. At the same time, the news that Italian troops are approaching the border of French Somaliland has caused concern here. However, well-informed observers are very skeptical about whether French territories will be involved. It is reported that French troops are now being sent to Djibouti in French Somaliland to strengthen defenses there, but they will not arrive until the beginning of next week. (Reuters dispatch on the 3rd)

(Paris) This newspaper's diplomatic correspondent has learned that diplomatic circles are not expressing surprise at the outbreak of the East African war and are now considering taking economic and financial sanctions to shorten the war. The first step is to prohibit loans to Italy; the second step is to prohibit the transportation of goods to Italy. The complete blockade of Italy will be decided at a later date. In other words, it will be implemented only after the League of Nations Executive Council unanimously decides and the Abyssinian war has not ended. This is because Article 16, paragraph 1 of the League of Nations Covenant stipulates that once the Executive Council designates the nature and severity of the aggression, it will choose among the various sanctions. Diplomatic circles here believe that the initial sanctions adopted will be milder measures and that more drastic measures will be adopted only after these measures have been tested for a long time and deemed ineffective. It is generally believed that once this procedure is adopted, it will not cause international disputes, because Italian Prime Minister Mussolini's speech yesterday and the guarantees provided by the Italian Ambassador to France Cerruti to Prime Minister Laval both stated that Italy would not strongly resist economic sanctions, and the British government is only considering collective action and does not want to take any action alone. (Havas dispatch on the 3rd)

(Paris) It is reported that the current negotiations between the British, French, and Italian governments are mainly aimed at making the East African conflict localized and not involving the European region. The general impression is that European war and Mediterranean disputes can be avoided for the time being. It is reported that Italian Ambassador to France Cerruti reiterated to French Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval yesterday that the Italian government will not take any aggressive action in Europe first and will strictly adopt a defensive posture in the Mediterranean. If the League of Nations sanctions are limited to economic and financial measures, Italy will not take any steps that would harm European countries. (Havas dispatch on the 2nd)

(London) Regarding the issue of sanctions, officials believe that only two kinds of economic sanctions can be adopted: one is to prohibit arms to Italy, and the other is financial sanctions, and the third is to boycott Italian goods. Regarding financial sanctions, that is, refusing to lend long-term and short-term loans to Italian countries, groups, or individuals. Regarding boycotting goods, it is generally believed that 60% of Italian exports are purchased by member states of the League of Nations. The United Kingdom accounts for 11%, France and Switzerland account for 8%, and the remaining member states account for 41%. In addition, non-member states, namely the United States, account for 9%, and Germany also accounts for only 9%. Therefore, if the League of Nations decides to prohibit its member states from purchasing Italian goods, it will naturally hinder Italian export trade and reduce its financial resources. Although this method may not take effect immediately, the East African war can be ended sooner, and there will be no disputes with non-member states. (Havas dispatch on the 3rd)

(Rome) Italian Undersecretary of State Suvich received French Ambassador to Italy Chambrun this afternoon. (Havas dispatch on the 2nd)

Roosevelt Reaffirms U.S. Neutrality; Reviews Naval Maneuvers

San Diego President Roosevelt, in a speech at the California Pacific Exposition today, reiterated the U.S. resolve to remain neutral in the event of war elsewhere, saying many Americans are uneasy, fearing some countries will repeat the foolish acts of twenty years ago, and the result will be the fall of culture to the extent that global restoration is impossible. Such fears are not unfounded. Whatever happens overseas, the U.S. not only wants peace, it is extremely anxious to avoid dangers which might damage its peace with the world. (Reuters dispatch on the 2nd)

San Diego President Roosevelt, in a speech here today, affirmed that regardless of what happened overseas, the U.S. must maintain neutrality and freedom, and that Americans deeply feared war would destroy world civilization and make global restoration impossible. The American people are passionate about freedom of religion and equality under the law, and so cannot tolerate the enforcement by other countries of laws violating these principles. This remark by the President clearly targets the German National Socialist government. Regarding the issue of U.S. restoration, the President said the government would not permit deflation and wanted to rebuild on this wreckage. He also intended to explore policies to raise prices, especially agricultural prices, as this was a prerequisite for industrial recovery. The President continued by saying that the nation's people were not anxious to return to the gold standard. (National Telegraph on the 2nd)

Flagship Houston Before departing for a tour of the Panama Canal today, President Roosevelt reviewed the largest-scale naval exercises in U.S. history at the San Diego naval base. Under the command of Rear Admiral Butler, 400 naval aircraft took to the skies, unfolding the prelude to the exercises. A total of 130 warships and submarines participated in the exercises. (National Telegraph on the 2nd)

Berlin Observers: Germany Will Also Maintain Neutrality; Official Opinion Not Yet Announced

(Berlin) Official circles here are now closely watching the situation between Italy and Abyssinia. It is rumored that the League of Nations intends to ask non-member states to express their attitude on this case, so the masses are paying more attention to this matter. The opinions of official circles have not yet been revealed, but it is expected that Germany will abide by Hitler's declaration made near Nuremberg that Germany does not want to intervene in events that are not related to it. At the same time that news of the Italian military's invasion of Abyssinia reached here, Hitler was staying in Tannenberg, and it is expected that he will return to Beijing earlier. (Reuters dispatch on the 3rd)

Belgian Prime Minister Announces Strict Adherence to the League of Nations Covenant; Visit of German Representative Has No Political Meaning

Beijing Belgian Prime Minister Theunis today in the joint meeting of the Foreign Affairs Committees of the Senate and House of Representatives announced that the Belgian government is now able to strictly adhere to the League of Nations Covenant, that is, the Locarno Treaty, and declared that the visit to Beijing by German Head of State Hitler's special envoy for disarmament, General Ribbentrop, has no political meaning. When talking with him, he only touched on general issues. According to reports, after Ribbentrop's recent visit to Beijing, rumors arose that Ribbentrop had suggested to the Belgian government to conclude a treaty of non-aggression between the two countries. (Reuters dispatch on the 2nd)

Italy Exercises Total Mobilization; Mussolini's Speech; Audience in Front of the Palace No Less Than 100,000

(Rome) Tonight, Italian Prime Minister Mussolini stood on the platform of the Palazzo Venezia to address the crowd. The secretary of the Fascist Party led 10,000 party members to line up in front of the palace to listen. When Mussolini spoke, the number of people gathered in front of the palace was no less than 100,000, and the number of people listening through wireless radio was even more unknown in the millions. At the same time, the British Embassy was closely guarded by 300 fully armed military police, and the Abyssinian Embassy was located in the suburbs of Rome, and its surroundings were also stationed with three layers of troops to prevent accidents. Mussolini previously stated that at this time, 20 million people across the country were happily listening to his remarks. He then said that Italy died 600,000 people and injured millions in the European War, helping to achieve the common victory of the Allied countries, but the spoils of victory belonged to other countries, and Italy only got the remainder. France should not forget the Italian soldiers who died in battle. He did not believe that France would now be willing to participate in sanctions to protect barbaric countries, but Italians must not ignore the possibility of sanctions. We will respond to economic sanctions with spiritual discipline, to military plans with military plans, and to war actions with war actions. However, Italy will do its best to ensure that the conflict in the colonies does not expand into a conflict in Europe. The audience in front of the palace applauded thunderously at this point. The Italian Prime Minister continued, "Today, those who are advancing towards their destination are not only the troops, but 44 million Italians are also united in hatred and advancing with the troops, because some people are trying to inflict very dark injustice on Italians and take away the little land they deserve. The Italians waited patiently for 20 years, and now someone is trying to inflict austerity on the Italians and block their vitality. Let others not think that they can make the Italians submit. The Italian people have never shown their spiritual strength and character power as they do now. The Italian people are the nation on which mankind relies to achieve its greatest victories, that is, the nation of poets, soldiers, and artists. Now someone dares to speak of sanctions against this nation!" At this point in his speech, the Italian Prime Minister became agitated and said, "Do I entrust the victory of Vittorio Veneto and the Italian Fascist Revolution? Let it rise quickly! Let our people convey their unwavering cries and determination to our soldiers in East Africa to give them comfort and security!" Finally, Mussolini announced that the national Fascist test mobilization had ended at 7:00 tonight. Mussolini did not explicitly mention the start of the East African war in his speech. As soon as the speech was over, the audience cheered for the Italian Prime Minister under the guidance of the secretary of the Fascist Party and then dispersed. (Reuters dispatch on the 2nd)

British Conservative Party Annual Conference; Advocates Expanding the Navy; More Than 2,000 Delegates Attend

(London) The Conservative Party held its annual conference in Brighton today. Representatives from various party associations attended, totaling more than 2,000 people. The first day of the conference focused almost entirely on debating the resolution proposed by Craig and Churchill, advocating that national defense be built to the extreme, regardless of the amount of expenditure. After the audience listened to the speeches of Churchill and Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain, they unanimously passed the case. Before the debate began, the audience cheered in favor of the motion proposed by Congressman Brigadier General Sir Croft, congratulating the government on the general policy of restoring commerce and finance, which has achieved progressive victories, and urging the active expansion of this political initiative. Party leader, Prime Minister Baldwin, will conclude the meeting tomorrow. Several other resolutions will be considered at tomorrow's meeting, one of which opposes ceding British territory to foreign countries without first obtaining the consent of the local British, and another which calls for special efforts to revive the suffering areas. When Churchill proposed the national defense case, he said that the major shortcomings of the national defense forces should be repaired immediately, especially for organizing various industries to quickly use them for national defense, and to renew efforts to make the British Air Force equal to the strongest air force country within a significant distance from the British coast. This is the responsibility of the government. Churchill also urged the government to rebuild the British fleet and strengthen the military to protect Britain's food sources and living needs, and to maintain the unity of the British Empire. Chamberlain replied that there was no need to remind the government to pay attention to its responsibilities to the country in defense matters, and the government had already started to handle everything described in the resolution. He also said, "Now, if everyone is willing to disarm, then we are also willing to disarm, but if others do not engage in disarmament, we must fill the gaps in defense so that the country can obtain security and maintain the empire, and fulfill our obligations to other countries. We are not supporting the League of Nations for this reason. We support the League of Nations because we believe that we can use the League of Nations to eliminate wars and lay the foundation for peace through collective action. If the League of Nations cannot do this, then it will not fulfill the task we hope for. Before abandoning the only hope that seems to be laying the foundation for a permanent peace in the world, we must be sure that the League of Nations really cannot do this." The Chancellor of the Exchequer then touched on financial matters, saying that our responsibility is first to guarantee security, and then to consider the issue of national wealth. (Reuters dispatch on the 3rd)

Page 6

National Legislative Yuan Roundtable: Invitation to German Ambassador for a Speech

(Nanjing) The Foreign Affairs Committee of the National Legislative Yuan invited the German Ambassador to China, Dr. Oskar Trautmann, to hold a roundtable discussion at the Yuan at 10:30 AM on the 3rd. More than 40 people attended, including Sun Ke, Wu Jingxiong, He Sui, Ma Yinchu, Chen Changheng, and Wei Tingsheng. Dr. Trautmann, accompanied by Counselor Lauterspil, arrived at the Yuan on time. After being received by Sun Ke with Chuan Bingchang accompanying him, he immediately joined the meeting. First, Fu Bingchang delivered an introductory speech, briefly stating that Ambassador Trautmann had a long history and rich experience in German politics and diplomacy. His presence at this meeting to report on the recent political, economic, and diplomatic situation in Germany would provide valuable information for our reference. Subsequently, Dr. Trautmann gave his report, which was translated by Zhang Pingqun, a counselor of the Executive Yuan. The report was divided into the following points, summarizing the political situation in Germany: (1) The political situation in Germany before Hitler came to power; (2) The process by which Hitler came to power; (3) The content of the National Socialist Party led by Hitler, further divided into three aspects: nationalism, socialism, and ethnic nationalism, to clarify its meaning; (4) Foreign policy. Finally, he hoped that after this roundtable discussion, Sino-German friendship would become increasingly cordial, and he said that the report mainly concerned the political situation of Germany's recovery after the European War. He also hoped that China could achieve great success in its own recovery. When Dr. Trautmann reported on foreign policy, he stated that German diplomacy was aimed at maintaining world peace. No matter what kind of diplomatic issues arose, they were resolved peacefully because Hitler had said that resolving diplomatic issues by means of war was not worth the loss. Regarding the German people of Austria, a fraternal nation, they shared common feelings and concerns. After France returned Saar to Germany, Germany and France had reached a mutual understanding. Amicable relations with the Netherlands could also be gradually strengthened. Since the establishment of a maritime agreement with the UK, a new path had been embarked upon. Relations with Russia were more complicated, but Germany's eradication of the Communist Party was entirely an internal matter, the so-called "sweep the snow from your own doorstep, and don't worry about the frost on your neighbor's roof." Russia should understand this point. The rest was not mentioned. After Dr. Trautmann finished his report, Cheng Zhonghang, Wei Tingsheng, and Chen Changheng raised questions about Germany's discrimination against the Jewish people and the conscription and management of markets. Dr. Trautmann answered all of them. The meeting adjourned at 12:30 PM. Dr. Trautmann, his entourage, Chuan Bingchang, Ma Yinchu, Wu Jingxiong, He Sui, and the chairmen of the various committees went to the Sun Yat-sen Mausoleum to attend a banquet hosted by Sun Ke. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 2nd)

(Nanjing) German Ambassador Dr. Trautmann gave a speech at the National Legislative Yuan, first stating that after the European War, Germany had a multitude of political parties, and political power could not be developed. Under this kind of environment, as the saying goes, "a chaotic world produces heroes," and the savior Hitler emerged. The party program of the National Socialist Party under Hitler's leadership included: 1. Nationalism; 2. Socialism, seeking social understanding through national freedom and equality, used for labor-capital coordination. Hitler believed that internal stability was the basis for resisting external aggression, so he was determined to unify the whole country. Hitler said that lasting peace between countries depended on their own equality. Germany's withdrawal from the League of Nations was because it treated Germany unfairly, such as the limitations on armaments, which weakened Germany's ability to defend itself. Dr. Trautmann continued that Hitler's acquisition of power was entirely through legal procedures, but it could also be said to have been somewhat revolutionary. Hitler not only opposed the Communist Party but also opposed the parliamentary system. The German government took the interests of all 66 million German people as its own. Absolute restrictions were placed on the freedom of a few reactionaries, because it was impossible to give freedom to reactionaries and allow them to endanger the country and the nation. This was also what Sun Yat-sen meant when he said that seeking freedom and equality for China was not seeking individual freedom and equality. Therefore, German politics went from a multiparty system to a one-party dictatorship, and from a one-party dictatorship to a one-man dictatorship. When the German elections were over, Hitler was elected with 90% of the vote. Hitler was still not satisfied and said that if Hitler obtained 100% approval, then the task of German national revival would be able to advance. As for the laborers under the current situation in Germany, although the same laws are enacted and courts are established, there are very few labor-capital lawsuits, because they are coordinated. Even if there are small problems, they are not handled by the courts, but by labor arbitration. Labor unions have been abolished and replaced by the Labor Grand Alliance, standing on the same front as the capitalists to seek progress in production. This is what Confucius called benevolence and forgiveness, and the so-called "when food and clothing are sufficient, people will know propriety and righteousness." The German labor movement is carried out under this principle. Germany is also making every effort to plan the revitalization of rural areas. At present, the value of agricultural products is determined by the government, and it is implemented uniformly throughout the country. There is no such thing as waiting for a price to sell. Market management is implemented so that farmers can have sufficient supplies. In addition, there is a system of ancestral fields, that is, landlords have a limit on the mortgage and sale of land. All farmers who sell their fields must retain 40 to 50 mu of basic land and are not allowed to sell it, in order to stabilize the livelihood of farmers, which is also the meaning of "the tiller owns his land." Its name is the ancestral field system. Dr. Trautmann then described Germany's conscription system, saying that it allowed the unemployed to solve their livelihood problems. Germany is currently deeply concerned about the tragic situation of war, where one general succeeds while ten thousand bones are left to rot. It hopes for world peace and that unemployment can be gradually reduced. Therefore, Germany is investing in the construction of highways and the expansion of industry to solve the unemployment problem. According to statistics from the year before last, there were 6 million unemployed people in Germany. Through these efforts and methods, there are now only over 1 million unemployed people. General observation believes that it is not a good way for Germany to borrow money to carry out reconstruction projects. At present, Germany's short-term public debt amounts to 5.5 billion marks, some of which have been converted into long-term public debt. However, on the one hand, calculating last year's tax revenue, it increased by about 1 billion marks compared with the previous year. From this point of view, this increase in tax revenue should be the result of reconstruction projects. At present, the paper money issued by Germany, up to this year, amounts to 3.8 billion. In 1934, foreign trade still had a large deficit. In summary, Germany's foreign policy is to maintain world peace. All kinds of pending issues are hoped to be resolved peacefully, because resorting to war, even if it wins, will not help in practice. Germany shares weal and woe with Austria, a fraternal nation. The German people will never forget this. After Saar was returned to Germany by France, there is a good possibility of promoting true friendship. It is believed that Poland can calmly resolve pending issues. As for the UK, since the naval agreement was signed, it has embarked on a new diplomatic path. As for Soviet Russia, although Germany opposes communism, Germany has decided to take the attitude of "sweep the snow from your own doorstep, and don't worry about the frost on your neighbor's roof." All other issues are also aimed at peace, so there is no need to list them in detail. Finally, he wished China's reconstruction the greatest success. He then added that Germany does not have special discrimination against Jewish people. All Jewish people who served Germany during the war are still serving in the German government. He also said that under the conscription system, the government provides them with food and clothing, and pays them several yuan in salary in the first month. Your country's ambassador to Turkey, He Yaozu, recently visited Germany to observe the conscription system and said that China may promote it in the future. (Special dispatch from the 3rd)

(Nanjing) The National Legislative Yuan's regular meeting on the 4th will review and revise important bills such as the three types of railway regulations for private, specialized, and state-run railways, as well as the administrative litigation and appeal laws. In addition, the Yuan's Commercial Law Committee and other committees held a meeting on the afternoon of the 3rd to review and revise the trademark law, and invited officials from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to attend the meeting to provide explanations. As a result, the review must continue. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 3rd)

Northern Jiangsu Disaster Victims Exempted from Participating in Huai River Project

(Xuzhou) The Huai River Conservancy Bureau previously ordered disaster victims in northern Jiangsu to participate in the Huai River project. Commissioner Shao, citing many difficulties, telegraphed the provincial government for instructions. The disaster victims are scattered in various districts, townships, and towns. Participating in the Huai River project would require a long journey, taking a long time, and would require the district and township chiefs to be stationed at the construction site for management, which would shake the original baojia organization, which is impossible. If the conscripted laborers were to form another baojia organization, management would be unreliable. This is one difficulty. Since the number of people is large, protection is difficult to provide. To prevent accidents, at least two companies of security guards must be stationed at the construction site for supervision. Tongfeng Pei Pi is known for its many bandits. Since the disaster in western Shandong, bandits have often infiltrated the junction of Jiangsu and Shandong. The strength of the security forces is already thin. If security forces are sent to the construction site, winter defense will be even more worrying. This is the second difficulty. The above are the most difficult of the difficulties. Can the association be requested to take responsibility for all management matters after the disaster victims arrive, and to issue a portion of the wages in advance to pay for resettlement? If this is not allowed, in order to provide relief to disaster victims and implement public works, there are also many projects in this area that should be undertaken. Chief Technician Yu is currently drafting a plan to reorganize the western dike of Weishan Lake and dredge the Bulao River to prevent water disasters, which is very important. Can it be reserved for public works in this area to avoid various difficulties and to allow the disaster victims to obtain real benefits? Time is pressing, so I telegraphed to request your examination and speedy instructions. The Jiangsu Provincial Government replied on the 2nd, stating that since there are difficulties for laborers from the disaster-stricken area of the district to participate in the Huai River project, they are exempted from participation. Northwest Bandit Suppression Headquarters to be Established Soon

Zhang Xueliang Suspends Trip to Taiyuan

(Beiping) The Northwest Bandit Suppression Headquarters can be established in Xi'an in the near future. The organization is roughly the same as the former Henan, Hubei, and Anhui Bandit Suppression Headquarters. Its authority is to be responsible for commanding the troops of the five provinces of Shaanxi, Gansu, Ningxia, Qinghai, and Xinjiang to suppress bandits within their borders. It is not accurate that it will command the bandit suppression forces of the seven provinces of Henan, Hubei, Shaanxi, Gansu, Ningxia, Qinghai, and Xinjiang. Moreover, because banditry in the Northwest is very deep, there is almost a combination of civilians and bandits. Therefore, political work is also very important. In the future, it will still be carried out based on the principle of 30% military and 70% political. The headquarters will also increase the establishment of a logistics station due to the inconvenient transportation in the Northwest to facilitate transportation and handle everything. Personnel for the headquarters will be transferred from various departments of the Xingying. Some personnel have been ordered to depart from Wuchang for Shaanxi. The name of the Xingying will still exist in the future, but the scope will be reduced, and a small number of personnel will be left to handle the pacification affairs in the border areas of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui. The Army Reorganization Office of the Xingying will continue to work as usual. (Special dispatch from the 3rd)

(Beiping) The Northwest Bandit Suppression Headquarters appointed Zhang Zhengfang as the director of the Transportation Department to manage logistics and transportation work. (Special dispatch from the 3rd)

(Taiyuan) Zhang Xueliang telegraphed Yan and said that he is currently preparing to organize the Northwest Bandit Suppression Headquarters and that his trip to Taiyuan is tentatively suspended. (Special dispatch from the 2nd)

(Beiping) The Northwest Bandit Suppression Headquarters is roughly the same in organization as the former Henan, Hubei, and Anhui three-province Bandit Suppression Headquarters. Due to the inconvenient transportation in the Northwest, only one more logistics station has been set up to facilitate transportation. The bandit suppression area under its jurisdiction is the five provinces of Shaanxi, Gansu, Qinghai, Ningxia, and Xinjiang. All the officials of the department are transferred from the Xingying. Some of the officials have been ordered to leave Wuchang for Shaanxi to prepare everything. It is expected to be established soon. In the future, it will still be based on the principle of 70% political and 30% military of Chairman Chiang Kai-shek to work hard to suppress the bandits. It is heard that except for the personnel of the Army Reorganization Office of the Xingying, the personnel of the other departments will not be replenished after they are transferred. The rumor that the Xingying will be closed down is not yet the time. Because the Red Bandits in the three provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui have gradually been eliminated, but the pacification work has not yet been completed. Therefore, the main task in the future is to focus on pacification matters, and the organizational scope will be reduced accordingly. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 3rd)

(Qingjiangpu) Sun Ziping, the first foreman of the Huaiyin section of the Huai River Diversion Project in Yangzhuang Town, discovered that workers had dug up ancient porcelain teacups, teapots, rice bowls, and vegetable plates with white ground and blue patterns in the construction area of Xiaoyuzhuang at noon on the 2nd, a total of 28 pieces. He intended to take them for himself, which led to conflicts with the workers and the section chief Sun Anbang. Section Chief Wu Guoxian investigated and ordered all the ancient porcelain to be transported to the section office for safekeeping and further resolution. (Special dispatch from the 3rd)

Land Law to be Amended

(Nanjing) Although the Land Law has been promulgated, it has not been implemented. China Literature and Art Society Holds Board Meeting

(Nanjing) The China Literature and Art Society has been established, with Ye Chucang as the president, Chen Lifu as the vice president, and Zhang Daofan, Zeng Zhongming, Fang Zhongxiao, Tong Zhi, and 17 others as directors. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 3rd)

Special Donation for Superstitions in Fujian Province

(Fuzhou) The provincial government has approved a special donation plan for superstitions submitted by the Finance Design Committee. The donation tax section of the second department of the Finance Department is responsible for handling it. Based on the annual consumption of superstitious items in the province, which exceeds 5.5 million yuan, a 30% tax will be levied, generating approximately 1.1 million yuan annually. The collection scope is limited to four categories: firecrackers, paper money, incense sticks, and candles. After the implementation of this tax, existing donation methods for superstitious items in Ningde, Songxi, Yongchun, Jinjiang, and other counties will be abolished and replaced with this unified approach. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 3rd)

Interpretation of Ambiguities in Prison Regulations

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Justice, based on a request from the Shandong High Court, has issued an interpretation regarding ambiguities in Article 5 of the Provisional Regulations on Prisons. The interpretation is as follows: According to the current system, county magistrates who concurrently administer judicial affairs possess both trial and prosecutorial powers. In areas without courts and prosecutors, county magistrates concurrently administering judicial affairs have the authority to apply for rulings ex officio when cases with finalized judgments remain unexecuted or incompletely executed and meet the criteria for converting sentences into fines under Article 41 of the Criminal Code. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 2nd)

Capital City Newspaper Society Hosts Li Youjun

(Nanjing) The Capital City Newspaper Society held a tea party at 4 PM on the 3rd to host Li Youjun and invited him to give a speech on his observations of the newspaper industry in Japan. The event began with an introduction by Xiao Tongzi, the executive director of the society. Li then provided a detailed account of the current state of the Japanese newspaper industry. According to a survey conducted in 1923, there were a total of 279 newspapers nationwide, with 208 in Tokyo and 90 in Osaka, accounting for a quarter of the total. Major newspapers all publish evening editions and distribute local versions in important cities. In terms of circulation, the Tokyo Asahi has 1.1 million copies, the Tokyo Nichinichi has 1 million copies, the Osaka Asahi has 1.3 million copies, and the Osaka Mainichi has 1.2 million copies, making them the most widely circulated. Major newspapers have very complete equipment. For example, in addition to various printing presses, the Asahi Shimbun also has 19 airplanes, 500 carrier pigeons, and two telephoto machines. Furthermore, the Ministry of Communications has installed private long-distance telephones for them. Japan has two major news agencies, United News and Electric News, and there is a possibility of a merger in the near future. The government imposes strict restrictions on the establishment and management of new newspapers, but currently adopts a policy of freedom of speech. In terms of industry communication, there are the Newspaper Association, the Journalists Association, and various clubs. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 3rd)

Internal Affairs Ministry Assigns Personnel to Discuss County Magistrate Examination Measures

(Nanjing) Regarding the detailed measures for the county magistrate examination and the emphasis on academic theory and practical application in the examination, the Ministry of Internal Affairs has assigned personnel to discuss with the Examination Yuan. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 3rd)

No Stamp Tax Required on Bus Tickets

(Nanjing) The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce requested the Ministry of Finance to clarify whether stamp tax should be affixed to bus tickets. The Ministry of Finance ruled that bus tickets are a type of ticket and should be included within the scope of Article 3, Section 10 of the Stamp Tax Law, thus no stamp tax is required. Method for Official Correspondence Between National Tax Agencies in Various Provinces and County Governments

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance, upon the order of the Executive Yuan, issued the following three regulations to the senior national tax agencies in various provinces regarding official correspondence with county governments: (1) For the counties and cities under the jurisdiction of the provinces of Hubei, Hunan, Anhui, Fujian, and Jiangxi, where joint offices have been established, the senior national tax agencies should send official letters through the provincial government when assistance is needed. In case of emergency, in addition to sending official letters through the province, telegraphic or substitute telegrams may be used to notify the county and city governments to provide assistance. (2) For provinces other than the above five, the previously established method for official correspondence between county governments and national tax agencies shall continue to be followed. However, if joint offices are established in provinces other than the five, the first method should be adopted immediately. (3) When the senior national tax agencies need assistance from the bureaus under the jurisdiction of the municipalities directly under the Executive Yuan, they should send official letters to the municipal government for notification. The Ministry of Finance has ordered compliance. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 3rd)

—Special Cable from Reuters, October 13th—

Gold and Silver

US Dollar: The London gold price today is 141 shillings and 10.5 pence, up half a penny.

British Silver: In the London silver market, both India and China are buying, and the price is up by 0.0625, currently priced at 29 pence and 4375, futures at 29.5 pence.

Exchange Rates

British-American: In the London foreign exchange market this morning, Europe bought British pounds. The British pound opened at 4 dollars, 89 cents, and 75 mills, higher than the closing rate of the US and British yesterday by 0.125. At 11:00, it continued to fall by 0.0625. At 2:00 PM, it rose by 4.375 to 4 dollars, 90 cents, and 0125 mills.

British-French: The opening fell by nine pounds to 74 francs, 4. At noon, it rose by 10 pounds to 74 francs, 44, with no changes afterward.

Cotton and Wheat

US Cotton: The New York cotton market opened this morning, and trading was quite active. The Africa war is the main reason. The sharp rise in the price of cotton also boosted morale. The opening price was about 11 points higher. Then, due to covering sales, there was a slight reaction, but the market conditions soon became firm again.

British Cotton: The Liverpool cotton market was stable this morning. At 1:00 PM, the January futures price was 6.06, higher than yesterday's closing price by 15 points.

British Wheat: There were few sellers in the Liverpool wheat market this morning, and prices soared. At 1:00 PM, the December futures price was 6 shillings and 8.625 pence, higher by 2 pence and 2375.

US Wheat: In the Chicago wheat market, due to good reports from the Liverpool and South American telegraphs, the opening price rose by 75. Then, because the buying momentum was strong, the price continued to rise. The price of coarse grains opened and fell by 25. The market conditions were sluggish. Merchants seemed unwilling to be active until they received reliable news from East Africa.

Rubber

London: The London rubber market was unchanged at the opening this morning. The January and February futures price was 5 pence and 8125. At noon, it rose by 0.0625.

New York: The New York rubber price rose by 8 points at the opening. Later, due to a lack of short covering, the market price rose by another 2 points. Market conditions then turned quiet. The price at the time of the cable transmission was not much different from the opening price.

Securities

New York: Merchants were worried about the outbreak of the Abyssinian war. Wall Street opened this morning and was very choppy. The steel industry fell the most. The market price was turning stable, especially for mining stocks and steel stocks. However, the price of International Telegraph and Telephone stock fell by 125 compared to the opening price. Generally speaking, the price of the securities had a rising trend at the time of the cable transmission. The average opening price of the Dow Jones 30 Industrial Average was 127.58, a drop of 48 points. The various prices are as follows.
