Dedicated Articles

Criticism of Yan Xishan's Land Village Ownership

— Zheng

Mr. Yan Xishan, seeing the spread of the Red Peril, has generously announced a fundamental anti-communist plan, advocating land village ownership. His understanding and courage are truly admirable. In recent years, the central authorities and people in society have expressed that anti-communism must focus on cleaning up politics and economic transformation, but until now, they have not dared to have a clear reform plan, let alone explicitly say that the current land problem is the main reason for the prevalence of communist disasters. Mr. Yan, in his capacity as a local authority, from his years of political experience, can recognize the crux of the problem, and express his fundamental change to the existing social structure and economic foundation. His decisiveness is truly amazing.

However, Mr. Yan's proposed principles and methods are too general. From a scientific standpoint, we dare not blindly agree.

Mr. Yan's advocated land village ownership is similar to the Equal-field system (均田制) and Allotment system (口分制) of the Northern Wei, Sui, and Tang Dynasties in our country, and the Cultivated Field System (研田制) after the Taika Reform in Japan. This system also has some value in a purely agricultural society with vast land and sparse population, because it can break the boundaries of inequality and achieve the effect of equal wealth. However, the reason why the Equal-field system and Allotment system of ancient China and the Handen System of Japan eventually collapsed is that the harmony between man and land is extremely difficult, the continuation of management and control is too complicated, and the more advanced agricultural management and more complex social organizations of modern times do not allow its existence. Mr. Yan has forgotten historical facts and is still advocating this kind of medieval method today. Although his intentions are not to be criticized, it is ultimately not enough to be a land policy suitable for our country today.

Judging from Mr. Yan's outline of land village ownership methods, its main points can be divided into the following five points: (1) Land is taken over by the village with public bonds; (2) According to the nature of the land, it is divided into various unit areas and distributed to farmers for cultivation; (3) Farmers receive land and return land at the beginning and end of their cultivation age; (4) Immigrants regulate wide and narrow villages; (5) Various direct taxes are used to repay public bonds for buying land. Now, please discuss these five points separately.

(1) How the land is taken over by the village is not discussed for now, and how the advantages and disadvantages of land village ownership and private ownership are different has the value of discussion. In primitive societies, both in China and abroad, land belongs to the blood-related group of the village. Descending to the present day, both in China and abroad, a private ownership system must be produced on the land, because human habits and social institutions make it inevitable. Although human beings are the spirit of animals, they are still one of the animals. The selfishness of animals has not disappeared in human beings so far. The normal development of selfishness is to seek the full, appropriate, and happy survival and the maximum display and continuation of vitality under the condition of not hindering the survival of others. Therefore, human beings began to store civilization and have society. The root of all civilization cannot but be based on the development of human self-consciousness. Therefore, some people call the concept of ownership a great invention of human society, because with the concept of ownership, there is the concept of economy, so human beings can start to work diligently and with hard work to seek their livelihood. If one person's strength is insufficient, the family's strength is used to do it. If one person's body is insufficient, the strength of sons and grandsons is used to do it. Therefore, human beings are increasingly breeding and becoming rich. Human society can exist and develop. The reason why the concept of private ownership is criticized is that it is overdeveloped, and eventually harms the public for private gain and harms the lives of the public for the benefit of one person. If we can correct public and private affairs and use a more perfect and thorough system to prevent its malpractices, then we can decisively judge that private ownership is better than public ownership under today's civilization process. This theory is true in other aspects, and there is an undeniable truth in terms of the land system, because the natural habit of land requires human blood to cultivate before it can be developed and promoted. The more dedicated and loving people are to the land, the greater its productive capacity should be. Intensive management all originates from the small farmer self-cultivation system, while nomadic systems and large landlord systems, or bad tenant farming systems, result in a weak relationship between land and people, and a lack of love. The productivity of the land is obviously reduced. The collective management advocated today, although has a solid basis in management skills, is ultimately difficult to hope for universality, because the love between people and land is not as deep as private ownership. Therefore, in terms of land management, the consciousness of village ownership is ultimately not as beneficial as the consciousness of private ownership.

In modern times, the nature of land has been financialized, and exchange, trade, gift, and inheritance can all represent its value as a unit. The establishment of this land price is the main reason for the evolution of modern village economy into a national economy. All the inherent properties of land, and the labor and capital invested by humans, can be expressed in a uniform monetary unit nationwide. Therefore, land has general economic properties, and humans can individually increase or decrease the land they own at any time according to their living needs and cultivation ability. Looking at Mr. Yan's method, although the land is still paid for by private management, it is advocated to be owned by the village, then the land must be prohibited from buying and selling transactions, then not only the economic properties of the land are completely lost, but the people cannot control it according to their needs. In the end, it is what is called using people to sacrifice the land, and using the land to tie people's lives. The serfdom of the Middle Ages will be revived. Regardless of whether it cannot be tolerated by the recent economic system, it is also not permitted by the facts of today's human society. Today, human life and death are uncertain, gathering and dispersal are impermanent, and cultivation ability varies due to old age and disease. How can we ensure that the continuously increasing population can obtain the land it deserves? How can we take the surplus to compensate for the deficiency and make the cultivation ability and the amount of land suitable? These are all great difficulties in fact. The land allotment of the Tang Dynasty and the handen system of Japan could not prohibit the people from privately receiving and selling each other, and as a result, they returned to private ownership. This is the main reason. Therefore, to carry out state operation by state ownership, learning from Soviet Russia, although the benefit of land financialization is lost, it can still be forcibly argued. Now, to talk about village ownership and pay for private management is definitely a contradictory theory. This is because, in terms of land economy, village ownership is not as good as a perfect private ownership system.

Other problems, such as the instability of the village unit, the difficulty of village ownership management, and the many malpractices of the method of buying with public bonds, are the last details of the problem, so they will be abandoned and not discussed.

(2) Mr. Yan's ideal is that the land can be divided into units according to the various qualities and the farming capacity of one person. Mr. Guan does not know that the quality of the land, its water, drought, fertility, and barrenness, varies greatly, and the farming capacity of one person is also extremely difficult to estimate. Mr. Yan's intention is probably to seek a calculation method in general, without seeking its accuracy and fairness. However, how can this be said to be a national policy? All legislation must seek its precision and fairness, and then the world will obey, and the officials will have no way to manipulate the situation. If the legislation itself is already unfair, then the trend of the situation will inevitably lead to the world being restless. Mr. Yan also said that there will be great differences between villages due to the size of the scope, the number of people, and the fertility of the land. He forcibly explained it by saying, "People's pursuit of life is like water flowing downwards. Although the boundaries of the village are fixed, the residence and migration of people are originally free. One is fixed, and the other is active. Even if there is unfairness, it can naturally tend to be fair." Alas, how can this theory convince the world? If the villagers are allowed to freely migrate to seek a living, then the areas with fertile land, convenient transportation, and rich production in the world will flock to them like ducks. The occurrence of chaos will be immediate. If the villagers are content with their homeland and do not want to move, and would rather die old in their hometown, forcibly seeking a share in the area where they grew up, what method will Mr. Yan use to drive them like water flowing downwards? If the people can be like water flowing downwards and naturally tend to be fair, then the theory of wide and narrow villages will not arise when the Equal-field system is implemented, and the matter of doubling the fields in wide villages and halving them in narrow villages should not be seen in the records. This proposal is not only divided into different units, but the unfairness at the time of the initial distribution is especially serious. Even if it is occasionally implemented, it will inevitably lead to hundreds of malpractices, and the unfairness will become more and more severe, and it will eventually lead to the fate of natural abolition.

(3) Accepting and returning land, its spiritual defect is that the consciousness of private ownership is not established, making people's love for land weak, management is not dedicated, and production is reduced, as mentioned above, and the practical difficulty is that the procedures for accepting and returning are extremely complicated. If the household registration is lost, fraud will occur, because people have life and death, sharks move, and households have marriages, divisions, and combinations. Now, if we count the mouth and give land, and determine the acceptance and return according to age, then the ancient Tuanmao system has seen its end, and the current Baojia system is not enough. It is necessary for the European personnel registration system to be strictly enforced in poor and remote areas before the method of acceptance and return can be realized, but this is only the beginning. The population is increasingly breeding, there are few who return the land, and there are many who are waiting to be granted land. What will happen then? Mr. Yan's relief method is that the village office can re-divide according to the increase in population, but I do not know where the dispute of re-dividing the whole will go. After the re-division, the unfairness between this village and that village will be even more serious. Moreover, the second weight will come soon. Such a layer-by-layer re-division will lead to the disaster of fragmented land division without end, and the difficulty will never be broken through.

Today's agricultural population in China accounts for 80% of the total population, which has exceeded the proper percentage. If the national economy has the hope of recovery in the future, then the agricultural population must be gradually reduced, and the industrial population must increase day by day. Mr. Yan's theory is just the opposite, and will make everyone farmers, because the land village ownership system, although it does not force everyone to be farmers, but because farmers can get a share, which is more advantageous than being other entrepreneurs, with no basis at all and having to rely on their own efforts. The difficulty is not the same, who would not give up the difficult and seek the easy? Why not first have this share to seek a living? Therefore, even in terms of the entire national economy, Mr. Yan's theory is not acceptable.

(4) Immigration to regulate wide and narrow villages is not the main body of this method, but an incidental provision to help those who are poor in this method. However, in terms of immigration, it is also not easy. Being content with one's homeland and placing importance on migration is the habit of farmers. In one word of migration, the state does not know how much force it will have to spend before it can engage in it. After the migration, whether their living habits and farming skills are up to the standard is still unknown. In terms of the village conditions in our country, most of them live together as a clan. Moving people of clan A and living in the village of clan B is also not something that people can integrate without hindrance. From the central and southeastern provinces of our country, the population density between counties is not far apart, and it is extremely difficult to regulate wide and narrow villages. According to the results of various surveys in recent times, such as Zhejiang, Jiangsu, and Hunan and Hubei, all feel the lack of land. If the number of farmers is used to divide the land equally, there is still not enough two or three acres. How can we allocate shares according to farming ability? If we seek regulation in remote areas, whether the country has such strength today to carry out large-scale immigration is a big question. Moving people from the southeast to the remote areas, in terms of the current national treasury, is a problem that cannot be done. Therefore, this proposal is also only enough for reference, and not a valid method.

(5) Buying land with public bonds and repaying the principal in installments with the income from various direct taxes, the disadvantage lies in the credibility of the public bonds, which is irrelevant to land policy, so it will not be discussed for the time being. The disadvantage of the tax being added to the farmers themselves is that it harms the soundness of the policy itself, so we cannot but say a word about it. Land village ownership and granting land according to the mouth, and the result will inevitably lead to a uniform burden, which is a theoretical fact. According to Mr. Yan's proposal, the farmers will have to pay 10% of the tax in the future (10% of the harvest). This is several times higher than the current land tax, because the cost of agricultural management, seeds, cattle, fertilizer, agricultural tools, and other necessary capital usually accounts for 30% to 40% of the harvest. The cost of food and clothing throughout the year is only 60% to 70% of the harvest. Now, taking one of them again, it does not seem to be heavy at first glance, but after detailed calculation, we know that it is an unbearable burden. Mr. Wan Guoding, in his book "The History of the Chinese Land System", cited a section on the Equal-field system and fleeing households as evidence, "The Equal-field system equally distributes land to the people, but the most fleeing households are in the Northern Dynasties, Sui, and Tang Dynasties that implemented the Equal-field system. Is it that the people do not like to have land? No, the Han Dynasty did not grant people land, but levied taxes according to the mu, so the household tax was lighter. Since the Equal-field system was implemented, the land rent was also collected according to the household, so the household tax increased greatly. However, the acceptance and granting of land only happened when the politics was clear and there were more land and fewer people. It was only temporary when it was followed, and there were many times when it was nominal. Powerful people annexed land, and the poor and weak lost their way. The officials no longer granted land, but the tax that was levied could no longer be lightened. The heavy tax became a disease for the people, and they fled together, not because they hated having land, but because they fled the heavy tax. Therefore, the poor and weak were harmed in the name of granting land... Therefore, whether the Equal-field system is better for the people's livelihood than the Han or Song and Ming Dynasties is truly a question." This kind of opinion of knowledgeable people, and I have the same feeling about the system advocated by Mr. Yan. As for the trouble of collecting this kind of tax in kind, the loss, and the gains and losses in the national finance, there is no need to discuss them deeply.

The advantages and disadvantages of Mr. Yan's land public ownership method are roughly discussed in this way. Since the method itself has many obstacles and is difficult to be perfect, what is its anti-communist strength? It does not need to be judged. Moreover, it may be because it is drawing a tiger like a dog, which may arouse the people's communist consciousness, and there is no reasonable method to produce it. The Communist Party takes advantage of the interests and can take the opportunity to do harm. Is the communist land distribution movement in Jiangxi Province not similar to Mr. Yan's system? Therefore, we cannot but hope that Mr. Yan will be cautious in making a decision.

Today's land policy in China is best at the equalization of land rights advocated by Mr. Sun Yat-sen. I have repeatedly discussed it. His method is not only suitable for today's national conditions, but also in line with the future trend of the world. It does not abolish the benefits of private ownership, but can remove the abuses of private ownership. It does not take the name of public ownership, but can have the reality of public ownership. The law is simple and easy to understand, easy to implement and without malpractices. Unfortunately, the people of the country either cling to the status quo and are unwilling to believe in the price and follow it, or they like to talk high and make other proposals to seek fame and shock the world. They either regard the equalization of land rights as empty theory or regard it as mediocre and unremarkable, misleading the common people, which is a great sigh. Is there a magic method to prevent communism today? Yes, there is only to take the theory of equalization of land rights and believe in it and implement it vigorously. Not only is it to prevent communism, but also the great fortune of the entire economic transformation and national revival will be predicted from this.

The Reaction to the Connection of the Songjiang Intercity Road

The county road from Songjiang to Sijing in this county was previously handed over by the county government to the Shangsong Motor Company to build with advance funds, and the project has been completed and opened to traffic. However, recently, the plan to connect the north gate of the Songsi Road with the east gate of the Songhui Road is about to be realized. The houses and graves along the route are being demolished by the county magistrate. The local people say that the Dongmen Main Street is also on the list of expansion. If it is implemented, the city will be divided into two, and transportation and commerce will be affected. The people went to the county to petition a few days ago, but did not get a result. So they sent representatives Zhu Jiuwang and others to Beijing to petition the fellow villagers association in Beijing, asking them to preside over the matter. It is reported that the association has telegraphed the provincial government, saying, "According to Songjiang citizens Zhu Jiuwang and others, the original route of the Songsi Road was originally planned to end at the North Gate, but the motor company that contracted the road has designated the route to extend to the East Gate, causing a lot of damage to the people's houses and graves along the way. They have submitted petitions to the provincial government and the county government, asking for a ban, but have not received a reply. The company has recently started construction without authorization and forcibly demolished and moved. Please save them. It is believed that road construction should take into account both transportation and economy, and should maintain the original plan and stop the expansion. If the road really needs to be extended, the damage suffered by each owner should be evaluated and compensated by the local public group before construction can begin to show fairness. The righteousness is related to the hometown, and it is urgently transferred." "The following is omitted" Another telegram to County Magistrate Jin of the county government said, "The case of the Songsi Road extending to the East Gate has not been agreed upon by the people. A letter is being sent to local people and this association has sent separate telegrams to the provincial government. Before a proper solution is obtained, you should handle it with caution."

Wuxi

The Dispute Over the Silk Cocoon Detention Case in Xushe

The Wuxi Dacheng Silk Factory received more than 500 dry cocoons from the Guanxing Renter in this year's autumn cocoons, loaded them on ships and transported them to Wuxi. Unexpectedly, in Xushe, Jiang Rujing and others gathered the villagers by striking gongs, saying that the factory cut off the market, suppressed the cocoons, and forced the farmers, and detained all four ships of dry cocoons. At that time, the factory reported to the Wuxi Silk Factory Association and forwarded it to the Chamber of Commerce, and telegraphed the provincial government and the two halls of civil construction, requesting that security teams be sent to the township to suppress and escort the cocoon ships back to Wuxi. Chairman Chen and Ministers Yu and Shen of the civil affairs hall and construction hall successively ordered the magistrates of Yixing and Liyang counties to investigate the truth and quickly resolve it. However, it has been almost ten days now, and the cocoon ships are still detained. Zhang Jifang, the manager of the Dacheng Silk Factory, sent Ding to Yixing to contact the various parties, but did not get any results. The district heads of all districts in Yixing County jointly submitted a petition to the county government, appealing for the farmers, accusing the cocoon merchants of suppressing the cocoons and requesting strict punishment for the fraudulent acts to avoid the pain of exploitation of the farmers. The dispute is becoming more and more serious. The Yongtai Silk Factory received the autumn cocoons in Liyang this time, and the price was around 20 yuan. At the same time, the price in Daibu was about 27 yuan. The villagers thought that the price difference was too large, and that the price was deliberately suppressed, so they detained the cocoon ships and refused to release them. The stalemate is still unresolved.

Inaugural Address

— Ye Gongwei

When Cheng Tang dissolved the nets, living beings flourished; when Confucius kept away from the kitchen, the benevolent loathed killing. Thus, they showed that all beings are one and should not harm each other. When people have murderous thoughts, it is the beginning of disaster. To eliminate disaster, the only way is to stop killing. Moreover, the world is now full of difficulties, and the situation is changing. The coming of the great disaster is especially frightening. Therefore, this association convened a publicity conference on the day of the World Animal Day, and also held a membership recruitment to hope that benevolent people will come together and work together to promote the movement. We sincerely hope that gentlemen of the country will extend their love to all beings and make their benevolence widespread. We cannot express enough our heartfelt prayers.

The Relationship Between the Animal Protection Association and the International Community

— Ren Wei

Since the British Parliament passed the Animal Protection Act in 1822, for a hundred years, the kindness of animal protection has spread throughout the world, whether it is the United States, France, Germany, Austria, Italy, Russia, Japan, or other countries. All the fallacies of using animals by nature have gradually lost credibility, and even those who have always despised animals have gradually expressed sympathy. Truly, the compassionate people are all the same, and the former saints and sages are the same. Our country was the earliest to be civilized, and its politics was based on leniency, and its customs were based on benevolence and righteousness. It has always been known for its morality. Even for animals, although the Song Dynasty could not completely ban slaughter, it also had considerable restrictions, such as Tang opening the nets and Confucius fishing without nets and shooting without killing. Mencius heard the sound and could not bear to eat the meat, and the emperor did not kill cattle without reason, the doctor did not kill sheep without reason, and the scholar did not kill pigs without reason. They were all set as rituals. It is known that the ancient sages and sages of our country, although restricted by the circumstances of the times, did not completely equalize all aspects like the Buddhists. However, their bitter heart to kill less is better than killing more, and to gradually reach the inability to kill is clearly revealed. However, in recent times, most scholars are only dazzled by the alarming theory of Darwin's struggle for survival and natural selection, without deeply studying the supreme principle of animal protection that people in the world have recently vigorously promoted. They pick up their spit and abandon their essence. Not to mention the inherent benevolence and beautiful virtues of our country, everything has a downward trend that cannot be recovered. Even in terms of international trends, in this time when the world hates killing and advocates extending kindness to all beings in order to restore the disaster and eliminate war, we alone ignore it and do not protect animals because they are weak and can be bullied. Is it not violating the trend of the national team, falling into isolation, and making people criticize us as a nation that fears the strong and bullies the weak, and is barbaric and cruel? Recognizing this, the associates have established the Chinese Animal Protection Association in order to reduce the suffering of all animals, transform the fierce atmosphere of grievances into auspicious aura, and at the same time cultivate the virtues of the people of the country, restore the inherent civilization, and cooperate with the benevolent and kind people of all friendly countries. The boundaries of people have disappeared, and the boundaries of nations have naturally disappeared. Using this to seek the great unity of the world and gradually reach the supreme rule of moderation and growth, this will not only be the fortune of the animal kingdom, but also the gospel of all mankind. Alas, the five turbid rivers are deep, and there is pain of sinking in the heart; the karma of sentient beings is heavy, and there is no clear shining in the nature. Protecting animals is also the essential effort to protect our heart and nature. Even the powers that have always embraced imperialism have recognized the crisis in the world and have this kind and gentle act of cultivating the mind. Our country has always emphasized benevolence and righteousness, but it is the opposite. Is it not a great shame? Alas; it can be revived.

Brief Description of Association Affairs in the Past Year

— Guan Jiongzhi

Since the association's proposal for preparation to its establishment, it has been two and a half years. The initial work was reported selectively at the Animal Festival last year. In the recent year, thanks to the enthusiastic support of people from all walks of life and all members, the various tasks of the association have not been slightly stagnant due to the prevalence of disasters and the insecurity of society. After all, disaster relief and resettlement of refugees are temporary measures, while promoting love and correcting people's hearts are the way to govern. Therefore, we have increased our efforts and are determined to proceed. Now, we will briefly describe the affairs of the past year separately below.

(1) Organization My country has a vast territory, and the situations in various places are quite different. It is inevitable that there will be regrets that the whip is beyond reach if we want to promote the cause of protecting life. Therefore, according to the planned plan, we have widely established branches. Those that have been formally established include Xi'an and Xijing (Chang'an) in Shaanxi Province, and those that are being prepared include Beijing, Changsha, Suzhou, Rugao, and Dongtai. It is estimated that they will be established in order soon. At the same time, in order to consolidate the strength of the association, we will start recruiting members today to gather ideas and benefit from each other, and work together.

(2) Propaganda The wind of cruelty in recent human beings has become a deep-rooted phenomenon, which is enough to hinder the promotion of the cause of protecting life. Therefore, the association's propaganda matters must strive for universality in order to arouse the attention of people from all walks of life. In the spring of this year, we negotiated with the Xinwen newspaper to publish a special issue on Protecting Life. Currently, three issues have been published, and we will continue to do so in the future. In July of the summer, the association printed 10,000 Protecting Life paper fans in response to the needs of the times and distributed them to people in this city, which was warmly welcomed by all walks of life and was exhausted within ten days. From April 8th to 13th of this year's Animal Week, the association assisted the Local Association for the Prevention of Cruelty to Animals (established by Westerners) to collect more than 2,000 animal protection paintings from children in various primary and secondary schools in this city and held an exhibition, which also gave the citizens a deep impression.

(3) Career In view of the pollution of the pond water on the Jiuqu Bridge in the Town God's Temple in this city, and the fact that many fish died, the association, in March of the spring, worked with the municipal authorities to set up pumps to remove the sewage and replace it with clean water. Small fish were also eaten by fish and turtles every day, and methods were devised to extract them and release them separately. At this year's Animal Festival, the association telegraphed the Ministry of Interior in advance to order all provinces and cities across the country to ban slaughter for one day in order to promote the protection of life, which was approved by the Executive Yuan. In addition, according to reports from members and people from all over the country, we appealed to local governments to ban the killing and eating of cattle and field chickens, and to stop the killing of wild dogs, the slaughter of pregnant sheep, and the upside-down of chickens, etc., all of which were handled separately.

The above are all major points. In addition, there are many matters to be handled, and we still need to proceed step by step. As for future plans, we have decided to set up animal treatment centers and organize burial teams in the near future in order to reduce animal suffering and maintain hygiene. We sincerely hope that benevolent people at home and abroad will give us guidance and support us with strength so that we can see its success as soon as possible, which is not only the fortune of animals.

Protective Words on Animals

— Shuang Yan

Today is Animal Day, designated by various countries around the world. The Animal Protection Society of this city has published this special issue to make everyone understand the meaning of animal protection. When this special issue was being edited, the editor-in-chief asked me for a contribution, and I couldn't refuse. So I wrote what I could say below.

I remember Mr. Yuan Jianzhai having a few words, saying that heaven produces living things to provide for people's mouths and stomachs. We humans slaughter and cut them up, wanting them to die is permissible. But to want them to die and yet make it impossible for them to seek death, that is not permissible. This is a level below what Mencius said, "Seeing them alive, one cannot bear to see them die; hearing their cries, one cannot bear to eat their flesh." But it still does not lose the benevolence in a person's heart. It would be great if we could avoid killing living things altogether. If we cannot, we should still not lose this benevolent heart. How can we subject animals to ropes and chains, whip them, and make them grieve and wail, making it impossible for them to seek death?

Buddhism prohibits killing, which is a benevolent heart. This benevolent heart is the same throughout ancient and modern times, both in China and abroad. Extending it to benevolence towards people and love for things, this heart is invariably the same. Humans are born between heaven and earth and are no different from other animals. Therefore, treat both self and others equally. One who can love animals can love people. Otherwise, destroying one's own kind is merely the same as having a cruel heart. Therefore, those who whip animals, kill to satisfy their appetite, drive people, seize land for private gain, and force them onto the chopping block and into boiling cauldrons, amidst the flames of cannons and aircraft, are all evil demons of the world.

If people were subjected to imprisonment, the torture and cruel punishments of prison guards, and all kinds of cruelties, they would invariably cry out to heaven and find no way to enter the earth, filled with grievances and anger, longing for death but unable to attain it. At this time, if you reflect on other animals, suffering innocent whippings, tight bindings, and pain, your heart should also feel desolate and pity them.

The Words of Animals

— Shu Chu

Besides all plants in the world, there is the world of animals. Human beings are a part of the animal world, which is recognized by everyone. The words of humans can also be said to be the words of animals, so I use these four words as the title of my article.

I saw in a newspaper report that Dr. ×× of × country used a certain live animal for medical experiments, performing live dissections. Also, Dr. ×× injected poison into the limbs of a certain live animal to cause changes in the venom and make discoveries. If you ask him why he used live animals for experiments, he would undoubtedly answer that it's because the physiology of animals is the same as that of humans. Then I can't help but ask him, aren't your children the same as animals? Why don't you use your children for dissection or experiments? It can be seen that humans are indeed the most cruel and selfish of animals.

My friend Mr. Shen Shiwan, for the purpose of protecting animals, talked to me about abstaining from meat and fish, which is indeed of considerable benefit to the body and mind. People who love to eat fish and shrimp harm hundreds and thousands of lives with each meal. It is better for a hundred or so people to share a cow. I couldn't help but retort that, in terms of minimizing the taking of life, it is indeed slightly better for a hundred or so people to share a cow. However, the cow has toiled for people in farming, and it can be said that it has nourished the lives of a hundred or so people. Not repaying its kindness is already unfeeling. Now, eating its flesh makes humans an unbearably cruel animal. If one were to seek such behavior in other dull animals, I'm afraid they wouldn't be found. Mr. Shen lowered his head and remained silent for a long time after hearing this.

City Party Headquarters Passed Resolutions at Yesterday's Regular Meeting Regarding National Day Celebration Methods – Grand Celebration Meeting to be Held at the People's Education Hall – All Agencies and Organizations Should Also Commemorate Individually – The Whole City Should Display Flags and Banners and Observe a One-Day Holiday –

October 10th is the 24th anniversary of the founding of the Republic of China. The City Party Headquarters of this city, in preparation for the celebration, has drafted commemorative measures, which were approved at yesterday's Standing Committee meeting. The measures are as follows: (1) Convene representatives from all sectors of Shanghai to hold a National Day commemorative meeting. (2) Date: October 10th, 10:00 AM. (3) Location: Southern City People's Education Hall. (4) Meeting Staff: Presidium, City Party Headquarters, City Government, City Farmers' Association, City General Labor Union, City Chamber of Commerce, City Education Association, City Returned Women's Association. (5) Masters of Ceremonies and Reception: To be handled by the Publicity Section staff; Security: To be handled by the Adjustment Section staff. (6) Starting from the 8th of this month, announce in the newspaper for three days. A. All agencies, organizations, and schools will have a one-day holiday on this day. In addition to sending five representatives to attend the meeting, they should also hold commemorative meetings separately. B. All agencies, organizations, schools, shops, factories, and residences in this city should display flags and banners on this day to show their celebration. (8) Meeting promotional materials, letters to the public, slogans, and banners, and the meeting order will be determined separately.

Loan for Domestic Goods Factories Due at the End of October – Ministry Approves Accommodation

The Shanghai Domestic Goods Factories United Association received a document from the Ministry of Finance, Qian Zi No. 7330, regarding the long-term loans of various Shanghai banks and firms, which are due at the end of October. The document requests that the Ministry order accommodation for rollover periods to extend the lifeline of factories and avoid bankruptcy, and also order the Bank of China, Bank of Communications, and the National Industrial Bank to be responsible for handling industrial and commercial mortgage loans to avoid shirking responsibility and provide relief. The Ministry acknowledged receipt of the request and approved forwarding the request to the Shanghai Banking and Currency Guild to request its members to clear interest payments and accommodate rollover periods for loans due at the end of October. The Ministry also stated that Shanghai industrial and commercial mortgage loans should still be handled in accordance with the Ministry's current loan principles. The order was issued to the Shanghai Banking and Currency Guild and should be noted.

Currency Guild Held an Executive Committee Meeting Yesterday – Elected He Zhongxiao as Chairman – Recommended Candidates for the Bank of China Inspection Committee

The Currency Guild held its first executive committee meeting of the third session at 2:00 PM yesterday at the Ningbo Road headquarters. Attending committee members included Wang J眉mei, Zhang Mengzhou, Zhang Wenbo, Xu Wenqing, Lu Shuchen, Chen Lishan, Xi Jiming, Shao Yanshan, Shen Jingliang, Liu Wuqiao, Zhao Songyuan, Zhang Dafu, and others, totaling twelve. Absent were He Zhongxiao, Yan Dayou, Zheng Bingquan, and others, totaling three. Shao Yanshan was publicly elected as the temporary chairman, and Ge Huaiqing, the secretary, recorded the minutes.

Election of Standing Committee Members: The proceedings were conducted in accordance with protocol. After the chairman reported the number of attendees, standing committee members were elected. As a result, He Zhongxiao, Xi Jiming, Shao Yanshan, Liu Wuqiao, and Lu Shuchen were elected as standing committee members. Subsequently, a chairman was elected from among the standing committee members, with He Zhongxiao, representing Zikang Village, being elected. Xu Wenqing was appointed as the Director of General Affairs, Zhang Dafu as the Director of Finance, and Zhang Mengzhou as the Director of Investigation.

Resolutions on Various Cases: After the elections, the committee began discussing proposals. (1) Regarding the letter from member Cunde Heji Village reporting a slight change in shareholders, with Xie Lian selling half of his shares to Jiang Heqin, resulting in Jiang Tongdetang Qiji holding six and a half shares, Jiang Heqin holding one share, Jiang Fengyuantang Zhuji holding half a share, Feng Ruidong holding half a share, Xie Jianting holding half a share, Zhang Rongzhou holding half a share, and Zhang Wenbo holding half a share, with the brand name and manager remaining the same, the committee resolved to approve the proposal. (2) Regarding the letter from valuation committee members Zhang Mengzhou, Xi Jiming, Lu Shuchen, Feng Yigui, and Liu Wuqiao, stating that the valuation committee should be dissolved because the regulations of the reserve fund had been revised and approved, and the highest authority of the reserve fund was now the general meeting of basic members, the committee resolved to decide after the executive committee of the reserve fund had been selected. (3) Regarding the letter from former committee member Wang Huailian, stating that he wished to resign from his positions as the Bank of China inspection committee member, the Sino-Foreign Banking and Currency Industries Joint Committee member, the primary school board director, the city chamber of commerce representative, and the tax-paying Chinese association representative, the committee resolved to publicly nominate Liu Wuqiao and Zhang Wenbo as Bank of China inspection committee members and requested Wang to continue in his other positions. (4) Regarding whether to announce the holiday on the 10th of this month (National Day) in the newspaper, the committee resolved that it was unnecessary and that the announcement should be posted in the market. (5) Regarding setting the date for the internal trading, the committee resolved to hold it at the guild headquarters at 2:00 PM on October 25th. The meeting adjourned around 4:00 PM.

Letters to Various Organizations: The guild, having elected the executive committee, standing committee, chairman, and representatives to various organizations, not only reported to the party and government agencies and notified various guilds and firms, but also sent letters to various relevant organizations. The original letter stated: "Respectfully informing you that our guild held a general meeting of members' representatives on October 2nd for the second re-election of officers. Under the guidance and supervision of personnel from the party and government agencies, eight executive committee members and five alternate committee members were elected in addition to the seven incumbent members. They were sworn in on the same month and held the first executive committee meeting of the third session on the 3rd, electing five standing committee members and then electing a chairman from among the standing committee members. In addition to reporting and sending notices, we are enclosing the list of committee members of the third session. Please take note of this. With best wishes. Shanghai Currency Guild. Attached is the list of committee members of the second session: Chairman: He Zhongxiao; Standing Committee Members (5): He Zhongxiao, Xi Jiming, Shao Yanshan, Liu Wuqiao, Lu Shuchen; Executive Committee Members (15): He Zhongxiao, Xi Jiming, Shao Yanshan, Liu Wuqiao, Lu Shuchen, Chen Lishan, Yan Dayou, Zhang Mengzhou, Zheng Bingquan, Wang J眉mei, Xu Wenqing, Zhang Dafu, Zhang Wenbo, Shen Jingji, Zhao Songyuan; Alternate Committee Members (5): Ye Xiuchun, Wu Zilin, Qin Zhensu, Tian Zixin, Zhang Shanshu."

Continued Repayment of Train Purchase Advance by the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway

The Shanghai-Nanjing Railway owed the Sino-British Bank over 117,000 yuan for the purchase of trains. In September of this year, it was due to repay £9,000. The accounting office settled the telegraphic transfer rate with Old Zhongyong Foreign Firm on September 13th, converting one shilling six and sixteen-sevenths pence into one yuan, totaling 117,152.54 yuan. On September 28th, the railway transferred the full amount from its reserve fund to HSBC, for remittance to London.

Request to Refund Import Tax on Artificial Silk Rejected by the Ministry of Finance – Due to Connection with Domestic Silk Industry Relief

The Shanghai Silk Guild previously noted that the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry were planning to follow the example of European and American countries by refunding a portion of the raw material tax within a possible range for goods sold overseas if the raw materials were purchased from overseas and the import tax rate was indeed too high, in order to encourage competition with foreign goods. The guild believed that China's silk industry had been popular worldwide. Since the import of artificial silk, it has been widely used due to its special effect of being dyed in two colors, and sales have been smooth. However, the import tax is very heavy. In order to reduce costs and expand the market, the guild specifically requested the Ministry of Finance to refund the import tax on artificial silk. The Ministry replied that it was related to the relief of the domestic silk industry and could not be approved. The Ministry replied to the guild, stating that the request to refund the import tax on artificial silk was related to the relief of the domestic silk industry and could not be approved. The reply was issued on September 27th, 24th year, by Minister Kong Xiangxi.

American Ambassador to China, Johnson, has been in Shanghai for several days. He is scheduled to return to Peiping by train at 4:00 PM today. According to what he told guests, he plans to come to Shanghai again on the 15th of this month to welcome American Secretary of War Dern and Vice President Garner. Secretary Dern is expected to pass through Shanghai around the 20th before going to the Philippines, and will make a trip to Nanjing. Vice President Garner and others will not go to Nanjing and will only stay in Shanghai for about 24 hours, so they will not have time to go elsewhere.

Xu Kan, Chen Xing, and Others Visited Song Together Yesterday – Discussed Expanding Rural Lending, etc.

According to Xin Xin News Agency, Vice Minister of Finance Xu Kan, General Manager of China Construction Bank Song Ziliang, and Deputy Governor of the Central Bank Chen Xing visited Song Ziwen, Chairman of the Board of Directors of the Bank of China, at the Bank of China at 10:00 AM yesterday, and left after about half an hour. They then went to the Central Bank to see Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi for instructions. According to a Xin Xin News Agency reporter, Chen and others visited Song yesterday because they believed that since Finance Minister Kong's efforts to rescue China's finances, people's hearts have stabilized and the market has gradually become stable. With the exception of areas affected by floods, all areas are celebrating a bumper harvest. It is now the autumn harvest season, and the Shanghai financial community plans to expand lending to rural areas and other sectors to promote social and economic activity.

Economic Observation Mission to Japan – Various Parties Hosting Banquets – Minister Kong Hosted a Banquet Yesterday Afternoon, Six Organizations, Including the Chamber of Commerce, Hosted a Banquet Last Night – Tonight, the Japanese Chamber of Commerce Jointly Hosts – Mayor Wu Hosts a Tea Party Tomorrow

The members of the economic observation mission to Japan, along with accompanying experts, secretaries, and family members, a total of 17 people, led by mission leader Wu Dingchang, are scheduled to depart from Shanghai on the Shanghai Maru on the morning of the 6th. Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi hosted a banquet yesterday afternoon, and six organizations, including the City Chamber of Commerce, hosted a banquet last night. The Japanese Chamber of Commerce and Industry, the Japanese Textile Industry Association in China, and the Japanese Banking Association will also jointly host a farewell banquet at 6:00 PM this afternoon at the Rokusan Garden. Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng will host a tea party at his private residence on Haige Road at 4:00 PM tomorrow afternoon. The details are as follows:

Minister's Banquet: The Minister of Finance hosted a banquet for the mission at 1:00 PM yesterday at the Central Bank on the Bund. Mission members present included Wu Dingchang, Song Hanzhang, Huang Wenzhi, Chen Guangfu, Zou Minchu, Zhou Zuomin, Qian Xinzhi, Yu Zuoting, Liu Hongsheng, Zhong E, Xu Xinliu, Hu Yun'an, Huang Yuequan, Kui Yao, Zhu Shuwang, and Secretary General Liu Tiecheng. Xu Kan, Chen Xing, Zhang Gongquan, Song Ziliang, Ye Zhuotang, Tan Zhonghui, Xi Demao, and Hu Mengjia accompanied them. The banquet ended at 2:00 PM, and Minister Kong then discussed matters with the mission members in the Standing Council Room until 2:30 PM. It is said that the discussion was about Sino-Japanese economic issues. A reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency met Rong Zongjing after the meeting. According to Rong, he has not yet decided whether to go to Japan due to health reasons.

Six Organizations' Banquet: At 8:00 PM last night, six organizations, including the City Chamber of Commerce, Local Associations, Banking Association, Shipping Guild, Currency Guild, and Press Association, hosted a banquet for the mission at the International Hotel. Those present included mission leader Wu Dingchang, mission members Xu Xinliu, Song Hanzhang, Chen Guangfu, Zhou Zuomin, Qian Xinzhi, Yu Zuoting, Tang Shoumin, guests Tong Hangbai, Jiang Huaishu, and Ke Ganchen, Chen Zeqing from the City Chamber of Commerce, Wang Yansong, Zhang Pei from the Banking Association, Xu Wenqing, Zhao Songyuan from the Currency Guild, Du Yuesheng, Wang Xiaolai from the Local Associations, and Yan Duhe, Tang Shichang, Zhu Xuefan from the Press Association, totaling more than 30 people. Yu Qiaqing and Du Yuesheng gave farewell speeches, stating that the economic observation mission to Japan bore a very important responsibility and hoping that they would conduct practical investigations for the country and the people. Mission leader Wu Dingchang then gave a reply speech, expressing his gratitude to the organizations. Finally, Yan Duhe gave a speech on behalf of the press, and the gathering dispersed.

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, Chen Zhaoying, Special Commissioner of Party Affairs of Fujian Province and Inspector of Zhejiang and Fujian, arrived in Shanghai at 3:20 PM yesterday on the China National Aviation Corporation's Shanghai-Guangdong line "Fujian" aircraft from Fujian. After disembarking at Longhua Airport, he went to his relative Zhang's residence on Moore Road to rest. Municipal Downtown Railway - Scheduled to Open on Double Tenth Day - Interconnecting Train Arrangement Determined - Fares Specially Reduced for National Games Service

The two Railway Bureau's municipal downtown railway (i.e., the Sanmin Branch Line) has been completed. After satisfactory trial runs, it will open on Double Tenth Day due to the Sixth National Games being held in the downtown area on that day. An arrangement for interconnecting trains, as well as timetables and fares, has been determined. Special trains will be operated on the Jinghu (Beijing-Shanghai) Line and Huhangyong (Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo) Line. Details regarding the branch line are as follows:

Operating Procedures: The Sanmin Branch Line connects to the Songhu (Shanghai-Wusong) Branch Line at the 6.5-kilometer mark. All operating equipment for the Sanmin Branch Line will be installed before Double Tenth Day. Temporary operating procedures for the interconnecting trains of the Sanmin Branch Line and the Songhu Branch Line have been established by the Traffic Department as follows: (1) At the connection point of the Minlu Branch Line and the Songhu Branch Line at the 6.5-kilometer mark, a temporary station will be established, tentatively named "Sanmin Road Junction Station." At the terminal of the Minlu Branch Line, a temporary station will be established, tentatively named "Sanmin Road Station." (2) When trains operate between Baoshan Road and Sanmin Road, the existing electrical road tokens and copper-iron road token system between Jiangwan Station and Gaojingmiao Station will be temporarily suspended. All trains traveling between Jiangwan Station and Sanmin Road Junction Station, between Minlu Road Junction Station and Gaojingmiao Station, and between Minlu Road Junction Station and Minlu Road Station, will use the copper-iron road token system, handled in accordance with the regulations of the operating rules. (3) The temporary copper-iron road tokens mentioned in the preceding article, for each section, shall be sealed and kept by the Jiangwan Stationmaster before use and after suspension of use. (4) The Sanmin Road Junction Stationmaster, taking the first Sanmin Road Branch Line train each day, shall proceed to the post. When passing Jiangwan, the stationmaster shall sign to the Jiangwan Stationmaster to receive all the copper-iron road tokens for the section between Sanmin Road Junction Station and Gaojingmiao Station, all the copper-iron tokens for the section between Sanmin Road Junction Station and Minlu Road Station, and the switch key of Sanmin Road Station. (5) The Minlu Junction Stationmaster, taking the last train of the Sanmin Road Branch Line back to Shanghai each day, shall properly lock the switch plate away from the Songhu Branch Line, extinguish all oil lamps, properly hand over the station equipment and sundries to the railway police for safekeeping, and carry:

the copper-iron road tokens for the section between Minlu Road Junction Station and Sanmin Road Station, and between Gaojingmiao Station and Minlu Junction Station, along with the switch key, and deliver them to the Jiangwan Stationmaster for inspection and receipt. He shall also obtain a receipt from the Jiangwan Stationmaster as proof before leaving the post. (6) The Jiangwan Stationmaster shall be responsible for telegrahically notifying related parties of the time and train number for each section to begin using the copper-iron road token system, as well as the time and train number to resume the electrical road token system, and report a copy to the Traffic Department Director and the Su-Song Section Traffic Section Chief. (7) After the Jiangwan Stationmaster properly hands over all the copper-iron road tokens for the section between Minlu Road Junction Station and Gaojingmiao Station, and between Sanmin Road Junction Station and Sanmin Road Station, and the switch key of the Sanmin Road Junction Station, to the Second Minlu Road Junction Stationmaster, he shall immediately telegraph notice to change to the copper-iron road token system. After receiving back all the copper-iron road tokens and the switch key of the Sanmin Road Junction Station, and verifying them without error, he may send a telegraph notice to restore the electrical road token system between Jiangwan Station and Gaojingmiao Station. (8) During the time that the Songhu Main Line and the Sanmin Road Branch Line have interconnecting trains, all trains passing through the Sanmin Road Junction Station must exchange road tokens or road signs. (9) Before the installation of the in-and-out station signals and switch signs of the Minlu Road Junction Station and the Sanmin Road Station, when trains approach each station, they must sound the whistle, reduce speed, and follow the hand signals shown by each station. (10) Since the Sanmin Road Junction Station does not have a passing track, during the time when the Songhu Branch Line and the Sanmin Road Branch Line have interconnecting trains, when trains travel from Jiangwan Station to Gaojingmiao Station, or from Gaojingmiao Station to Jiangwan Station, before entering the section, the Jiangfeng Station, Sanmin Road Junction Station, and Gaojingmiao Station stationmasters shall notify and consult each other, ensuring safety and punctuality.

Scheduled Times: The Jinghu Railway Sanmin Road Branch Line passenger special train schedule, from October 10th to October 20th: Downbound, Baoshan Road to Sanmin Road: Baoshan Road Departure: 8:05, 8:50, 9:35, 10:15, 10:55, 11:40, 12:20, 13:05, 13:45, 14:30, 15:10, 15:50, 16:35, 17:20, 18:00. Sanmin Road Arrival: 8:32, 9:21, 10:05, 10:45, 11:25, 12:10, 12:50, 13:35, 14:15, 15:00, 15:40, 16:20, 17:07, 17:55, 18:35. Upbound, Sanmin Road to Baoshan Road: Sanmin Road Departure: 8:50, 9:30, 10:12, 10:45, 11:35, 12:20, 13:00, 13:45, 14:25, 15:10, 15:50, 16:35, 17:20, 18:05, 18:40. Baoshan Road Arrival: 9:25, 10:05, 10:48, 11:30, 12:10, 12:55, 13:35, 14:20, 15:00, 15:45, 16:25, 17:10, 17:55, 18:40, 19:05. The above schedule includes 15 upbound and 15 downbound trains daily, stopping at both Jiangwan and Tiantong'an stations.

Fares: Both railways, to serve the National Games, have added the Sanmin Road Branch Line to the Songhu Branch Line, running passenger trains directly to the venue from Baoshan Road Station during the National Games to transport attendees. (1) Branch line fares are selectively reduced. Baoshan Road Station to Sanmin Road Station ticket prices: A. One-way ticket: 15 cents. B. Same-day round-trip ticket: 25 cents. C. Student group same-day round-trip ticket: 20 cents. Eleven-day period pass: 2 yuan. (2) Extended Round-Trip Ticket Validity: The validity period of round-trip tickets for sightseeing along the line, except for Hangzhou-Nanjing and Nanxingqiao-Nanjing, which is ten days, is originally seven days for other stations. Now, to facilitate participation in the National Games for people along the line, the validity of all round-trip tickets from major stations to Shangbei Station is extended to fourteen days, allowing travelers to attend the National Games and tour Shanghai at their leisure. (3) Fully Enhancing Travel Convenience: During the period, the railway has specially printed handbooks for passengers' reference. A service office will be set up at the National Games venue to sell train tickets between Baoshan Road Station and Sanmin Road Station, as well as tickets for each station on the railway. During and around the Games, inquiries regarding travel matters can be directed to the information center and sales office, which will provide detailed answers. For entrusted travel matters such as booking hotels, transferring luggage, designing itineraries, and purchasing sightseeing round-trip tickets, inquiries can also be made at the railway labor union information center or station.

Eurasia Company's No. 160 Aircraft - Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday by German Ship - To Fly the Shanrong Route After Assembly - No. 52 Aircraft Scheduled to Arrive at Longhua on the 8th

Eurasia Aviation Corporation ordered a JU60 Junkers small aircraft from German Lufthansa. It arrived in Shanghai around 3 PM yesterday aboard the third express vessel, the "Karl," of the North German Lloyd shipping company, docking at the Gonghexiang Wharf in Hongkou. The company plans to send personnel today to retrieve it and transport it by barge to Longhua Airport for assembly. It will be used to fly the Shanrong route. The aircraft is equipped with one engine, with a speed of 320 kilometers per hour, and can accommodate seven or eight passengers. As for the JU52 Junkers large aircraft borrowed from Lufthansa, in addition to the one that has already arrived in Shanghai, there is another one that was flown from Berlin by aviator Kaspar on the morning of October 1st, scheduled to land at Longhua Airport at 3 PM on the 8th. The aircraft is equipped with three engines, the same as the previous one. In addition, Mr. He En, the company's acting chief of the aviation group, has gone to Guangzhou to welcome the aircraft and accompany it to Shanghai.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Ship "Tonghua" Collides in Tianjin

Since last month, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's "Tonghua" has been rerouted to Lianyungang, Qingdao, and Tianjin, transporting cargo jointly from Laoyao (i.e., Lianyungang) and Tianjin, no longer coming to Shanghai. The ship left Tianjin yesterday morning heading east towards Shanghai. It was reported that the "Tonghua" was departing from the Zizhu Lin Wharf in Tianjin at 8:30 AM on the 2nd of this month, heading to Qingdao, when a tugboat suddenly rammed into the "Tonghua" in front of the Osaka Company Wharf. Fortunately, the "Tonghua" managed to avoid it, but the stern was still damaged. After inquiring with Shanghai, the ship has been instructed to unload its cargo and passengers and return to Shanghai for inspection and repairs.

US Flagship "Augusta" Arrives in Shanghai - Handover Between New and Old Admirals

According to the "Da Mei Evening News," the flagship "Augusta" of the United States Asiatic Fleet arrived in Shanghai on Tuesday (1st) afternoon from Qingdao. The ship, a 10,000-ton cruiser carrying 650 officers and sailors, plans to travel via Bangkok and Singapore to Manila. It will make a brief stop in Shanghai to await the handover ceremony of the Fleet Commander Admiral Upham. The newly appointed Commander Admiral Hepburn arrived in Shanghai a week ago and will assume office immediately after the handover from Upham. The handover ceremony is scheduled for 9:30 AM on Saturday (5th), with a very simple ceremony consisting only of the reading of the government's instructions to both admirals in front of the "Augusta" personnel, followed by an inspection of the entire ship. The "Augusta" is scheduled to leave Shanghai on October 8th for Manila for winter maneuvers. The black hawk, a warship with the American Asian fleet, left Yantai to head directly for Hong Kong, and several destroyers will accompany the "Augusta" on its southern journey. In January of next year, the US Asian Fleet will hold its annual routine combat exercise with the US Army in the Philippines.

Memorial Service for Mr. Li Shaochuan

Mr. Li Shaochuan, a revolutionary pioneer from Anhui, was born in Hefei. During the late Qing Dynasty, he advocated revolution and launched an uprising during the 1911 Revolution, restoring Hefei. He traveled to Fujian and Guangdong during the campaigns to protect the Constitution in Yulaiquan and other counties, participating in military affairs, advising on military strategy, enabling the Guangdong Army to return to Guangdong, expelling the Gui rebels, and laying the foundation for the revolution. His contributions were particularly significant. Throughout his life, he was benevolent, chivalrous, and sociable, befriending Zhu Zhixin, Deng Zhongyuan, Liao Zhongkai, Fan Hongxian, Zhang Mengjie, Zheng Zancheng, and other martyrs, as well as the current Chairman of the National Government, Mr. Lin Zichao, with whom he had a particularly close relationship. In recent years, he lived in seclusion in Shanghai, suffering from illness and worrying about the times. On June 26th, he suddenly passed away due to high blood pressure causing a cerebral hemorrhage. His comrades from near and far were deeply saddened. Mr. Xu Shiying, Bai Wenwei, Gao Yihan, He Shizhen, Guan Yunnong, Gao Yinzao, Chang Hengfang, Guan Shudong, Zhang Gongchen, Li Zhengqiu, Lu Yinan, and many other comrades from Anhui initiated a memorial service at the Huguo Temple in the racecourse yesterday, presided over by Shi Decun. Jin Weixi reported on Mr. Li's life, and Wang Lantian spoke about comrades from various places coming to Shanghai to attend the memorial. There were hundreds of attendees. Wreaths and elegies from Chairman Lin, Duan Qirui, Hu Hanmin, Sun Ke, Ju Zheng, Yu Youren, Xu Chongzhi, Ma Chaojun, Yang Hu, and others, as well as memorial essays by Gao Yihan and others, expressed deep sorrow. The scene was filled with sorrow, with cars and white horses coming and going in a constant stream, reflecting the honor of the moment.

Representatives of Dinghai Salt Farmers Arrive in Shanghai - To Proceed to Hangzhou Tomorrow to Petition the Salt Commissioner

According to the "New Voice News Agency," the salt farmers from the Daishan Salt Field in Dinghai County, who are responsible for the five salt kiln areas, have had their livelihoods cut off because the stipulated amount of salt for this year will not be subsidized. Over ten thousand salt farmers are in distress and panic, potentially leading to trouble. On the 28th of this month, the authorities convened a meeting of all salt farmers and invited Field Supervisor Tang and Salt Cooperative Secretary Zheng Xikun, along with salt farmer representatives Zhou Fengxian, Zhang Tongli, Liu Hekai, and shed leader Liu Lisun, to the Oushang Inn, rooms 91 and 92, to discuss the situation. After several rounds of consultation with Jian Chu, Chairman of the Zhejiang Salt Industry Association, and Yao Zhimei, manager of the kiln, no satisfactory results have been achieved. They plan to travel to Hangzhou tomorrow to petition the Liangzhe Salt Commissioner.

The Eighty-Third Batch of Expelled Overseas Chinese from Japan Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday - Xu Kangfa and Three Others

The eighty-first batch of expelled overseas Chinese from Japan, Xu Kangfa (from Ruian, Zhejiang), Jin Chengyi, Wang Jinlian, and Liao Maohan (from Yongjia, Zhejiang), arrived in Shanghai yesterday afternoon at 3 PM aboard the Japanese Postal Steamship Company's Tsukuba Maru, lodging at the Laogongxin Inn in the Sixteenth Ward. According to the Japanese newspaper reporters accompanying the refugees, they worked as coolies in Japan, earning only a few cents a day, barely making ends meet. Having been expelled and returning to China penniless, they plan to appeal to the Overseas Chinese Affairs Bureau for assistance in finding work at the Qiaole Village to make a living.

Lawyers Association Reports on Resolutions of the Judicial Conference - Matters of Common Interest to Lawyers

The Republic of China Lawyers Association sent a letter to the lawyers' associations of various provinces, reporting on the resolutions of the recent National Judicial Conference convened in the capital regarding proposals submitted by the legal community. The content of the original letter, in which the resolutions passed by the conference and submitted to the Legislative Yuan for review, is as follows: "The judicial conference's lawyer representatives held a meeting in Nanjing on September 10th and elected Liu Liumin, Jin Zhaowen, Jiang Yiping, Xiao Buyun, Zhang Siwei, and Zhang Tao as representatives to the National Judicial Conference. According to a report from Representative Liu Liumin, among the proposals submitted, the proposal to urgently implement a compensation system for wrongful convictions was resolved to be sent by the Judicial Yuan to the Legislative Yuan. (2) The proposal to urgently modernize the lawyer system was resolved to be sent to the Legislative Yuan along with the draft lawyer law prepared by the Judicial Administration Department. (3) The proposal to allow lawyers to practice in county governments that also administer judicial affairs was resolved to be passed in principle and referred to the Judicial Administration Department for consideration and handling. The above cases are of common interest to lawyers and are hereby communicated to your association for your information."

Zhabei Water and Electricity Company Supplies Electricity to Dalu New Village

The electrical users in Dalu New Village and Liuqing Small Residence on Scott Road were previously unable to obtain electricity from the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company, which held the exclusive franchise for the area, because the company's power lines had not yet reached the area. They had applied to the Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities for permission to temporarily connect to the Shanghai Electric Power Company, agreeing to switch over once the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company's poles and wires reached the area. Now that the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company's power lines have reached the area, the Bureau has notified the users in Dalu New Village and Liuqing Small Residence to switch over to the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company.

The Chinese Women's Temperance Union held its board meeting and annual meetings of various committees yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM at the union's headquarters. Over fifty people attended, including Mrs. Cao Yunxiang, Mrs. Lin Zhuoran, Mrs. Feng Xikang, Ms. Guan Cuizhen, Ms. Tang Qingyun, Mrs. Liu Tingwei, Ms. Xiang Wanqing, Mrs. Zhong Rongcang, and Ms. Cha Chen Hanxia. Ms. Wu Laoweiqing, the chairwoman, led the meeting through the formalities. The following proposals were passed: (1) The fifth solicitation campaign will be held from November 1st to 30th. (2) A board of directors will be established for the home school this year, and the Bureau of Education will be requested to register it and raise funds to build complete school buildings. (3) An advisory group for beggars will be organized, and the local authorities will be requested to provide relief. (6) Ms. Yang Meizhen will be appointed as representative to the United States, Mrs. Jiang Zuobin as representative to Japan, and Mrs. Guo Taiqi as representative to the United Kingdom. Finally, the directors were elected, and tea was served. The meeting adjourned in a happy atmosphere at 6:00 PM.

North German Lloyd's New Ship "Karl" Arrives in Shanghai on Maiden Voyage - After Arrival, Docks at Hongkou Gonghexiang Wharf - Will Depart for Japan Tomorrow Before Returning to Shanghai for Passengers

According to the Huadong News Agency, the "Karl," the third new giant express vessel built by the North German Lloyd shipping company, arrived in Shanghai yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM on its maiden voyage to the Far East, docking at the Gonghexiang Wharf in Hongkou. Details are as follows:

Arrival Situation

The ship sailed from Bremerhaven, Germany, on August 7th on its maiden voyage to China, stopping at the Netherlands, the United Kingdom, Portugal, Spain, Italy, Colombia, Singapore, Manila, and Hong Kong. Yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, it arrived off the Tongsha sandbar outside Wusong Estuary and was piloted into the Huangpu River by personnel sent by the North German Shanghai Company, docking at the Gonghexiang Wharf in Hongkou at around 4:00 PM. Passengers disembarked in succession.

Overview of the Entire Ship

A reporter from the Huadong News Agency visited the ship yesterday. The ship is similar to the company's "Scharnhorst" and "Potsdam" ships, with ultra-modern kitchens, swimming pools, sports grounds, condensing rooms, and artificial air conditioning in addition to bedrooms, reception rooms, and dance halls. Its capacity, speed, and cabin class are also the same as the above two ships. The entire ship's exterior is white, while the hull is black. The top floor is the machine room, and the swimming pool and sports ground are below. The ship was designed by the famous German engineer Bering, and its entire structure is extremely beautiful and magnificent.

Departure Tomorrow

According to information from the North German Company, the ship is scheduled to leave Shanghai tomorrow for Japan to pick up passengers, stay in Japan for two days, and return to Shanghai on the 8th to pick up passengers before returning to Germany. If time permits, prominent figures and journalists will be invited to visit the ship to understand the ship's facilities before it departs for Germany on a scheduled date.

Bureau of Inspection and Testing Entrusts Shanghai Bank to Offer Credit Loans to Employees

Total Amount Fixed at 15,000 Yuan, Assisting Employees with Legitimate Needs, A Model Agreement Established, A Pioneering Initiative

Cai Wuji, Director of the Shanghai Bureau of Inspection and Testing of Commodities, in order to support employees' legitimate purposes and financial needs, specially entrusted Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank to handle credit loans for employees. The highest amount of these loans is limited to 15,000 yuan. The terms of the loans were agreed upon by both parties at the end of last month, and the loans will begin this month. This type of loan is still unique in this city, and can serve as an example for other government agencies and commercial banks. Therefore, we have explored and recorded the full text of the agreement as follows:

Agreement

Shanghai Bureau of Inspection and Testing of Commodities (hereinafter referred to as "the Bureau") and Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank (hereinafter referred to as "the Bank"), in order to facilitate and mutually assist the Bureau's employees with legitimate purposes and small financial needs, have entrusted the Bank to handle credit loans for the Bureau's employees. The following five terms are agreed upon:

Terms

(1) Total Amount: The maximum total amount of the loans is fixed at 15,000 yuan. (2) Loan Amount: The loan amount for each person shall not exceed the individual's monthly salary. (3) Term: The maximum term shall not exceed six months, repaid in equal installments. (4) Interest: The monthly interest rate is six per cent, calculated monthly and prepaid upon the loan being granted. If the loan is repaid in full in advance, the unearned interest will be refunded based on the number of days. (5) Handling Fee: A handling fee of 25 cents per hundred yuan of the loan amount will be charged. For loans less than one hundred yuan, the fee will be calculated as one hundred yuan. (6) Repayment: The Bank shall, two days before the end of each month, provide a list of borrowers to the Bureau's accounting department, which shall be responsible for deducting the installments from the borrowers' salaries at the end of each month and remitting them to the Bank on the same day without delay. If there are any errors, the Bureau shall be responsible if the cause lies with the Bureau, and the Bank shall be responsible if the cause lies with the Bank. If a borrower leaves the job or is unable to continue service, and the amount owed to the Bank has not yet been repaid, the Bureau's accounting department shall be responsible for first deducting the amount owed from the borrower's remaining funds held by the Bureau, such as salary, savings, and other due payments. When a borrower leaves the Bureau's employment, if there are other outstanding debts owed to the Bureau, the Bureau, in order to protect the Bank's rights, shall first deduct the Bank's loan. (7) Procedures: When a borrower wishes to obtain a loan, they shall first obtain a "Installment Repayment Loan Form" from the Bureau's accounting department, fill in each item in the "Borrower's Service Status" section on the back, and submit it to the accounting department for signature and seal, then to the Bureau Director for approval, and then contact the Bank. If the signature and seal are inconsistent with the Bank's specimen seal, the Bank may refuse the loan. (8) Restrictions: If a Bureau employee has already borrowed a small loan from the Bank, the Bank, in order to accommodate the borrower's repayment ability, may revise the loan amount and term approved by the Bureau. (9) Guarantee: If a borrower is suspended from duty and unable to repay the loan, or if the accounting department fails to deduct the loan amount in full, the Bureau Director and the accounting department shall be responsible for guaranteeing repayment. (10) Supplementary Provisions: For matters concerning the loans stipulated in this agreement, if there are any matters not covered in detail in the preceding articles, the Bank's "Credit Small Loan Regulations" shall apply. However, Articles 2 and 3 of Article 10 of those regulations shall not apply. The Bank's Small Loan Regulations, with the Bank's seal affixed and approved by the Bureau, shall prevail.

Zhabei Public Bus Route 1 Changes to Shuishui Road

Effective on the 5th of this Month

The main line of the No. 1 route of the China Merchants Public Bus Company originally ran from Baoshan Road, Jiangwan Road, and West Sports Association Road to Jiangwan City. Now, in order to facilitate transportation to areas such as West Baoxing Road, Liuying Road, and Shuilei Road, the company has decided to change the No. 1 bus route from the intersection of Baoshan Road to West Baoxing Road, Liuying Road, Shuilei Road, and then return to the original line of East Sports Association Road, all the way to Jiangwan City, starting on the 5th of this month. The fare stages are as follows: from North Station to the intersection of Baoxing Road, nine copper coins; to Qingyun Road, twelve coins; to Liuying Road, sixteen coins; to Shidong Middle School, nineteen coins; to Chizhi University, twenty-three coins; to Yujing Temple, twenty-six coins; to the Livestock and Planting Company, twenty-nine coins; to the Racecourse and Jiangwan Town, thirty-five coins. It is heard that the fares for the entire line will remain the same.
