Reported to the City Council Leaders Meeting Yesterday　And Discussed Matters Related to Serving the All-China Games

The city scouts are scheduled to hold a flag-raising ceremony on October 10 to enhance the patriotic thinking of young children, awaken the national and state concepts of citizens, and commemorate National Day. The City Scout Council held a city council leaders meeting at the Minli Girls' Middle School on Wenmiao Road at 4:00 PM yesterday for this purpose. 123 council leaders attended, chaired by Leng Ranquiao, Standing Director of the Council, with Xie Yanbo as the recorder. First, the chairman reported on the flag-raising measures and important points to note. Then, Luo Lie, a director of the Council, reported on the mobilization of city scouts to widely donate to the flood relief preparation, and Zhao Weizu reported on the contact progress of the city scouts serving the All-China Games. The council leaders then successively expressed their opinions and introduced their wonderful service groups. Finally, Tong Hangbai, a Standing Committee member of the City Party Department and a Standing Director of the Council, gave a speech, mainly hoping to work hard in the cause, cultivate children, consolidate the national foundation, and promote national strength. After the speech, everyone had a cheerful meal together, which was a grand event at the time. The flag-raising ceremony measures and order are recorded below: (1) Flag-raising location: Municipal Sports Field in the city center; (2) Flag-raising time: 8:00 AM on October 10; (3) Number of participants: Each group is limited to two squads (18 people per squad, including the squad leader, who must be 16 years old or older); (4) Leader: The leader or trainer of the group; (5) Clothing and supplies: All participating scouts must wear single-split uniforms, shorts, black socks, black leather shoes, and carry batons and squad flags (group flags and military bands are not allowed to be carried, and the squad colors are uniformly used as shoulder straps); (6) Check-in time: Before 7:00 AM on October 10, deadline for late arrivals; (7) Check-in location: In front of the Municipal Government in the city center; (8) Assembly location: In front of the Municipal Government Square in the city center. Each group of squads will form four rows and be arranged in order of check-in by the command of the Council to enter the field; (9) Order: 1. Enter the field (arranged in a horseshoe shape), 2. Sing the Party Song, 3. Raise the flag, 4. Respectfully read the Premier's instructions, 5. Chairman's report, 6. Basic action exercises: (1) Attention, (2) Right dress, (3) Eyes front, (4) Right turn, (5) About turn, (6) Left turn, (7) About turn, (8) Support baton, (9) Baton down, (10) At ease. Note: Squad leaders and leaders of each group should still stand in place and do the actions for items 4, 5, 6, and 7 without moving. (7) Sing the Scout Song, (8) Ceremony concludes.

Little Men (65)

— Original by American author Louisa May Alcott, translated by Zheng Xiaocang

Fortunately, the dangerous situation was soon escaped. Mrs. Pei ordered the children to go back to sleep, leaving only the steward to watch out for a recurrence of the fire. Then she and Frang went to see how the unfortunate children were doing. Xiaoqiao only suffered a burn and a large scar. Taomo, not only did most of his hair fall out due to burning, but also had a large burn on his arm, which caused him so much pain that he almost fainted. They soon settled Xiaoqiao, Frang sent him to his own bed, comforting him so that he was no longer afraid, and even hummed a song for him like a loving mother, so that he fell into a deep sleep. Nasuiche took care of the poor Taomo, trying to reduce his pain. Mrs. Pei went back and forth between him and Xiao Tanddi, holding cotton, oil, and pain medicine in her hands, and often muttered to herself, as if she felt quite happy when she thought of this, saying, "I always knew that Tao Mo would set the house on fire one day, and now he has realized this sentence!"

The next morning, Mr. Zhuang came home and saw this mess. Taomo was trapped in bed, Tanddi was panting like a small whale, Mrs. Shu was extremely exhausted, and all the children were very nervous. When they saw him, they all wanted to tell him the story of last night, and they dragged him to survey the burnt field. He handled everything with a calm attitude, and everything gradually returned to order, because everyone felt that with him there, even ten big fires would be enough for him to handle, and everyone worked hard to do whatever work he assigned to them.

Four Million and Ninety Thousand in New September Coins

The Central Mint Examination Committee announced that the four million and ninety thousand yuan of new coins from the 23rd year examined in September of this year have been sampled and tested by the committee-appointed chemist Ge De in accordance with regulations. The composition and weight were found to be in accordance with the Silver Standard Coinage Regulations, and certificates have been issued from (22) 1764 to (23) 17881, totaling 808 certificates, allowing the coins to leave the factory.

Yarn & Cotton 非常涨風

Extremely Strong Upswing in Yarn and Cotton Prices Due to the Current Situation

The yarn market is experiencing tight conditions due to unrest. Overseas cotton markets are soaring, with high-quality yarns rising by 5 to 6 yuan and low-quality yarns rising by about 3 yuan. Market sentiment is boiling, with prices rising rapidly due to active sales and a lack of inventory for both coarse and fine yarns. The cotton cloth market is also experiencing special developments. The fundamentals of the yarn market are already strong. The labeled yarn market has been suppressed by the number of long positions taken last month to hedge this month, so even minor positive news is fueling an extremely strong price surge.

Golden Rooster Down 3.5 Yuan

Labeled Yarn Rises Sharply

In the morning session, labeled yarn prices opened with soaring prices for American and Indian cotton, boosting market sentiment. Prices for all months increased by 5.6 yuan. Long traders, encouraged by favorable news, aggressively added to their positions, while short traders scrambled to cover. Buying was extremely strong, and prices rose steadily, strengthening market sentiment. Prices continued to rise above the previous day's close, with gains ranging from 3 to 4.7 yuan. In the afternoon, continued strong sales of spot yarn and purchasing of 17- and 20-count yarns by the Sichuan traders, following Guangdong and others, prompted factories to sell almost all of their inventory, causing prices to continue to rise. Prices briefly declined by several jiao as some long traders took profits, but prices rebounded by the close, with a strong upward trend. Buyers included Dafeng (1,750 bales), Daji (800 bales), Zhenda (850 bales), Changchang (1,750 bales), Changfeng (950 bales), Tonghe (750 bales), Tongfu (750 bales), Taixing (600 bales), Runkang (650 bales), Yongda (550 bales), Yuan Yi (700 bales), Yi Chang (550 bales), Shen Yu (450 bales), Mingde (450 bales), Hexing (450 bales), and Yongchang (550 bales). Cotton

American and Indian cotton markets have been rising for days. Yesterday, the political news favored bullish sentiment, and prices rose another 35 to 44 pound-cents. The domestic cotton market is increasingly bullish. Short traders are eagerly covering their positions, while long traders are further adding to their positions, driving the market upward. As yarn factory inventories gradually run out, there is a potential for active consumption of raw cotton, further boosting bullish sentiment.

Labeled Cotton Rises Dramatically by 1.2 Yuan

Labeled cotton prices opened higher across the board, as external cotton prices rose sharply due to the potential for war in Europe and Africa. Prices for all months rose suddenly by 5.6 jiao. From the second session, market sentiment became even more bullish. Short traders, aware of the unfavorable situation, eagerly covered their positions, while long traders continued to add to their positions, causing the trading platform to become increasingly tight and prices to soar. The afternoon session opened with a more bullish market, as sales of spot yarn remained strong and there was potential for active sales of spot cotton. During the third session, due to a greater number of profit-taking closures, the price dropped a few jiao, but recovered by the close.

Astonishing News from Europe Stirs American Cotton Speculation, Market Price Sharply Rises Over Thirty Pounds

Yesterday, American cotton opened. Fluctuations across months reached four pounds. Near months softened due to increased hedging, while far months were driven by domestic and foreign peers joining in, coupled with astonishing news from Europe, attracting foreign states to cover shorts and speculators to enter. Weather was favorable, and Southern hedging increased, but it was absorbed. Subsequently, foreign merchants and the general public aggressively bought, pushing nine points, causing prices to surge. As a result, spot prices rose fifteen pounds, and futures rose three, six to forty-four pounds. English cotton spot prices rose points, futures rose points. Indian cotton futures traders and European exporters both traded actively, with slight hedging across markets. On average, Gul rose four point, Robi, Olmula rose five point five Robi, Bai Luoxi rose five Robi, original telegram (Reuters).

Grain: Italian-Albanian Mobilization Spurs Flour and Wheat Surge

The flour market presented another frenzied surge, with shore wheat prices in Chicago continuing to rise by one dollar, a considerable amount. Canadian prices rose by ninety cents. Market sentiment, due to the frequent surges in foreign wheat and the looming Italian-Albanian dispute, has shifted towards bullishness. Opening prices surged by three to four points, but later selling by major bulls eased the momentum slightly. However, the market surged again in the afternoon due to a Reuters telegram reporting a formal conflict between Italy and Albania, prompting widespread buying from both industry insiders and outsiders. Bids for all months aggressively rose. Given the seriousness of the international situation, future developments are bound to be disruptive.

Weather Clears, River Rice Arrives in Quantity, Prices Plunge

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, the sources from various locations were slightly more abundant than before, with over thirty arrivals in total (over seven thousand dan of goods). The weather cleared, and the sentiment softened, leading to sluggish sales in this street. Sellers lowered their bids, resulting in price drops of one, two, or even three jiao for thicker grains. Thinner grains from Yantai and Qingdao sold five to six hundred bags, with prices also dropping by a little over two jiao. Baige kiln varieties, due to extremely high inventories in recent days, experienced a sharp drop of four jiao, even though three to four hundred bags were taken in. Thick new japonica rice, being constrained, also exhibited a similar decline. As for new yangjian rice, its base was considered stable, but with waning sentiment, supply and demand became misaligned, leading to a price drop of two chi. Lujian rice was even more difficult to sell, with prices cut by three jiao, and old rice lost one yuan.

Recently, the exchange rate has been extended, and overseas silk prices have also gradually trended downward (New York is down four cents compared to last week, Yokohama is down fifty yuan). However, Shanghai manufacturers are still holding prices firm and are optimistic about the future, unwilling to sell easily. As a result, silk trading in Shanghai is reported quiet.

Tunxi Fine Eyebrow Tea Sells Actively in Europe

Tunxi Fine Eyebrow green tea has recently seen gradually expanding sales in Europe. Yesterday, firms such as Xiehe Jinlong Tongfu all purchased large quantities, with total sales of Fine Eyebrow reaching over one thousand eight hundred boxes across the city. The market opened at sixty yuan. In addition, transactions for Needle Eyebrow, Pearl Tea, and other items were also active. However, Wuyuan Fine Eyebrow, due to inconsistent quality and color variations, does not sell well in Morocco, and the market remains sluggish.

Metals: White Lead Sheet Prices Rise Again

Recently, there has been a shortage of incoming white lead sheets. Battery factories, printing houses, toy factories, and other buyers have all raised their purchasing prices by one or two yuan per dan. No. 2 is opening at twenty-six yuan, Nos. 3 and 4 at twenty-five yuan, Nos. 5 and 6 at twenty-six yuan and five jiao, and No. 7 and above are all opening at twenty-five yuan and five jiao. It is heard that recently, Nos. 5 and 6 have seen enthusiastic buying, with asking prices reaching as high as twenty-seven yuan.

Recently, incoming shipments of Tong'an sun-dried longan have been scarce, and merchants are showing great interest, causing the market to tighten daily. Free Talk

Children Also Need Books

— By Lin Side

Luther Burbank said: "Children like to play with mud pies, catch grasshoppers, crickets, water bugs, tadpoles, frogs, and turtles; pick elderberries, wild raspberries, acorns, and chestnuts; climb trees, play with water, fold lotus flowers; they are willing to do all these things. They love to catch gophers, bats, bees, butterflies, and all kinds of animals. Picking pine cones, rolling stones, scattering sand, slithering, and playing with bumblebees in the grass are things that no child has ever restrained themselves from, and restraining themselves from these things is like restraining a part of their good education." (Note 1)

To the things that Burbank proposed children should have, we can add one more point, which is that every child should have their books.

Finding fun in characters and taking pleasure in the sound of books has always been considered a kind of recreational activity. Reading is a tool for culture, and it has already been recognized by the world. It is necessary for education. However, 'education,' from the time we have had it until now, has never safeguarded the individual reading wishes of those receiving education. This is simply a bizarre contradiction. Speaking of valuing and using books, it often faces opposition due to the cultivation required, so some have said that only a small portion of adults actually read. Among them, the number of readers who can distinguish and find interest in ancient and modern texts is ultimately small. Even in the United States, which is known for its extensive education, according to the reading situation in 1926, "Out of 160 million people in America, there are almost 50 million readers, but most of these 90 million readers do not read other books besides the daily news and soft novels." (Note 2) The number of people who truly seek knowledge in books and appreciate profound literature is also extremely small. So now we know that to study children, we must find the importance and possibility of books in their young environment. We are not saying that we should often lock children indoors to pore over their dictionaries or push a Bible onto their seats, nor are we completely overturning their building of small houses to replace them with encyclopedias, but rather that from the time they can pick up their cloth-covered books, they are qualified to use their bookshelves and pictures.

If a child has the ability to dress, eat, and sleep alone, then naturally, they also have the ability to use their books. A child's dressing and sleeping naturally cannot be the same as those of adults, and even in terms of diet, it cannot be the same. Because they are infants, special care and nurturing are given to their genuine nature, and their physical development is strengthened and increased with time. Books and children, just like their beds, help them complete themselves, making them fully realized. That is to say, books can give children good and usable abilities.

Moore said, "Children must grow up from their books, and the selection of those books must be carefully considered in all aspects of life, while also matching the child's natural interests and never containing extravagant qualities. The most important thing is to pay attention to their mental and spiritual development and changes, just like giving them good food to maintain their bodies. In addition, we must also anticipate their purchasing power, that is, the value of the selected books must be within each family's budget." (Note 3)

What Moore said about choosing books for children should be "universal to people" is an excellent idea, but we still need to discuss the following: what methods do we use for the smallest children? How do we make two-year-olds use books? And how do we make books something a child can develop social and intellectual needs for? These are some questions.

To know whether a career is satisfying and beneficial, which is something we continue throughout our lives, the reading habits of adults, such as seeking knowledge and entertainment in books, are gradually learned and must be learned from the beginning for them to gain satisfying experiences from books. So, it is extremely obvious that if we want children to love books and hope to connect their lives with reading habits, then naturally we should provide them with this kind of progressive creative experience. However, among the currently popular books, who can judge which ones can provide to small children?

Speaking of children having some actions that are often annoying, they are often disliked by adults. In fact, these complex factors cannot be resolved simply by dislike. We still need to slowly teach them to do things. "For example, if we want children to hold books properly, it definitely requires an adult to kindly guide them." We see a child holding a splendid and pleasing book, sitting on a patch of green grass. The glossy pages rustle, and their skillful and discerning fingers draw blue, red, or yellow marks, (Note 4) how free and easy is that!

Children are extremely fond of books. Previously, there were two students in a nursery who spent a whole day looking at picture books, and their ages were about two and a half years old. One day, one of the children ran out of the room because of something, and as he got up from the chair and walked out, he suddenly dropped his book on the floor. Another child saw this and carefully picked it up, gently placed it on the table, and solemnly scolded the child, saying, "You can't do that; books are good things!" This kind of situation is solid evidence—and at the same time, we think of the expression that child emitted when he said those words, how meaningful!

But in reality, what can we do? In families, limited by budget and with several children, or with limited space or time, can we help children know what kind of books are "good things"? So the first important plan is that we must be able to dedicate time and money independently. Within our families, we must treat books as an essential part of a child's life and respect books and give books a serious place. This does not mean that we are dominated by books but rather that books have a limited place in our lives, like constantly using entertainment, knowledge, and abilities as tools. If we hold such an attitude, we will be worthy of our children. Walking into this kind of exemplary family, their respect for children can still suit the child's behavior. As for the child's fundamental necessities, they are naturally what parents plan for them. Like the purchase of those harmful books, there must be preparation in the family budget, equal to providing rooms for children to live in and allowing children to have entertainment time.

All of the contributions of these methods are that buying those books for children is not an overly wasteful request. It is hoped that inspiration like this will enlighten a child until they become an adult. Books are food for the child's body and wine for the spirit. Books can give them the right methods, have shared and friendly uses within the family, help their lives move from the boundaries of the family to the larger world, and provide them with life experiences that allow them to distinguish the taste of life. Therefore, even infants need books.

Note 1: See The Training of the Human Plant, PP. 91

Note 2: See Children's Reading PP. 3 by Lewis M. Terman & Margaret Lima

Note 3: See Seven Stories High,

Note 4: When reading books and newspapers, those sentences that feel satisfying or are unknown at the time can be marked with a horizontal line with colored pencils so that they can be easily found for recall in the future.

Water

— By Xiao Ge

There were six of them. After being stuffed with white liquor, they still had official business to attend to.

They walked staggeringly, still busy picking their teeth, unwilling to leave the chicken scraps in their teeth.

Their official business was to walk into a silk store.

"Where's the manager?" As usual, the old man always led the official business, and his three strands of beard added a bit of prestige.

"What do you want?" The fat guy stood up from the stool.

"We're apportioning some money for river works and tea water. Are you the manager?" The toothpick was dropped on the ground.

"N-no... but we've already hired river workers."

"Yes, yes, you've hired river workers, of course you pay them wages. But... but for the sake of the poor..."

"I say, is the flood coming or not?"

"No, no... so the poor folks who are assigned to work have no way, they have to eat, they also have to drink tea, so in our several baoli, we have to find a way to subsidize them. It's for everyone's sake, manager, isn't it?"

"But these days!" He gestured with his hand.

"These days, you don't want to live?" The young guy who came along was a bit fiery in his speech, and the old man gave him a look.

The manager didn't say anything.

"Didn't the first dike collapse?"

"Heard that × village has also been flooded!"

The shop assistants were most concerned about these things.

"Now, 100,000 laborers are working day and night to repair the second dike. × village only has two chi of water."

"If the water rises again, it'll be ruined!"

"Yes, so we still have to do our best. Manager, isn't it?"

The manager had already quietly sat down in the corner of the wall, and the old man walked over.

"Manager is..."

"So how much money do you want me to pay?" The fat guy shook his head on the chair.

"Five yuan, we're apportioning five yuan."

"Five yuan!" He stood up angrily.

"We have records."

He pulled out a few pieces of paper and spread them on the glass counter, but the manager didn't look at them, took a few angry steps, and said decisively:

"Baoli chief, you do the math for me, four laborers are assigned every day, four sixes are twenty-four, that's two yuan and four mao per day. You also want tea water, and what else, people can't afford it!"

"So are you paying or not?" The young guy got fiery again, and the veins on his red face swelled up a bit.

"How can people afford it?" He tilted his body.

"If you don't pay, we'll send you to the Public Security Bureau!"

"Public Security Bureau, good, let's go!"

The manager heroically walked to the door, but the old man caught up and grabbed him.

"Let's talk it over, let's talk it over. The young guys are just fiery tempered."

"I'm going, I'm going to get sued!"

The shop assistants all came forward to persuade him, and the fiery young guy hid at the door, roaring. A crowd of people gathered around to watch, it was very lively.

Another disturbance rose in the street.

A group of coolies walked by, and the one in the lead held a bamboo pole with a string of more than a dozen sugar ears on it.

"Everyone look, four people eating one !"

"We're not doing it anymore!"

"Spent other people's money, enjoying themselves."

"Damn his brother-in-law!"

A burst of shouting, the excitement in the silk store shifted to the street. The manager ran out the door first, looked around, and ran back in, bumping into the old man.

"What's going on? What's going on?"

The six of them caught up with a group.

"What's going on? Four people eating one ."

"I fuck your mother!"

"Who are you cursing?" The old man panted and struggled to keep up, unable to stop them.

"Cursing those brothers-in-law who spend other people's money and enjoy themselves."

"Nonsense! Outrageous! I'm going to take you to see the district chief."

"Good, let's go!"

The six of them and this group quickly walked away.

Character Splitting Stall

Honorary Old Woman (II)

— By Jiang Maxiu, Translated by Ren Jun

However, as I reflected on this influence, I couldn't help but feel afraid.

The events unfolded one after another. The situation in the Orient became urgent, and war finally broke out. General patriotic fervor, war fever, mobilization orders, expeditions... Military propaganda gradually became blatant. And it had a considerable effect. Suddenly, from the shadows of the screen, the sound of children singing in chorus to send off the soldiers came up. - In that instant, both my wife and I couldn't help but feel a chill in our hearts.

However, the general audience only had fanaticism.

After a while, the attacks on Lushun, the naval battle of the Sea of Japan, and the fierce battles of Fengtian unfolded. In these performances, the Japanese army had special forces open fire for backup, and the actors were actively active. I thought this was great. I even thought that although a few anti-militarists had tried to carry out various forms of resistance, preventing the influence of propaganda aided by the state was not an easy task.

Next, I felt as if I was experiencing the era of the Russo-Japanese War again. Because at that time, I was still a small middle school student in the countryside, and like the general public, I had been caught up in that dazzling and violent vortex of patriotic fervor and war fever. In fact, has there ever been a time when the people were more united in the fanaticism of patriotism and militarism than at that time? Now, watching this "Colonel Yoshioka" movie, I remembered the tension and fanaticism of the general public and atmosphere of twenty years ago, and I couldn't help but feel a kind of nostalgia.

However, my wife was much younger than me and did not live directly in that era. Therefore, she had no understanding of my emotions at all. And this "Colonel Yoshioka," especially the war scenes, she could only see the tragic, cruel, and disgusting things in them. Therefore, when leaving the cinema, she said that she really regretted not going home without watching this movie.

I didn't think her feelings were unreasonable at all. No, it was probably natural. However, as mentioned earlier, I had a kind of nostalgia for remembering that era.

The Birth of a Baby

— 仃

Before my wife went into labor, I had already started to worry. This, for us, was nothing short of a matter of life and death.

Our impoverished existence had long plunged us into a life of wandering and instability. Every day, we wracked our brains just to secure meager meals that barely filled our bellies. Every year, we racked our brains trying to find ways to obtain clothes that barely kept us warm. Despite exhausting all our life's strength to resist the onslaught of hunger and cold, we still ended up enduring hunger and freezing, and practically not a single day out of the 360 days of the year was a good one for us.

Sorrow and distress seemed to have become part of our daily lives.

We truly had an indescribable sense of melancholy regarding these unfortunate, difficult, and bleak years!

Now, what threatened me before my eyes was that my wife was about to give birth. For wealthy families, or people longing for descendants, this would be a joyous occasion.

However, for us struggling under the iron wheels of life, we felt no joy whatsoever. On the contrary, this matter made us even more immersed in anxiety.

My wife was giving birth for the first time, and because she had never experienced this before, she was particularly worried about her life. In the past, she had heard stories of difficult childbirths from the mouths of neighbors. Thus, the cruel image of death, the tragic impression of death, and the terrifying face of death had deeply penetrated my wife's pure heart, adding a layer of gloom to her life and leaving a larger wound.

I, too, had the same feeling. I did not think my wife's worries and fears were excessive. However, my wife's constitution was too frail, due to excessive labor and insufficient nourishment on ordinary days. This was obviously very unfavorable for her childbirth. I thought, how many unhealthy women in the world fail to pass through the ordeal of childbirth!

Thinking of this, I couldn't help but feel terrified and worried for my wife, and thus became anxious for her.

But, apart from worry, what good methods could we use to remedy the situation? This was as necessary as daily food and clothing. Could we stop that kind of natural human demand? Alas, the poor of this century are even deprived of a natural human pleasure.

My wife was very anxious because she was nearing labor. She dragged her heavy belly everywhere to find a solution. But after running around for several days, all our friends were as poor as us.

As for me, in the past, when I still had a job, if I was short of money in the middle of the month, I could still borrow from others. But now, it was no longer possible. They knew that we had no income and were poor, unable to repay debts, so they dared not lend to us with peace of mind.

So what should we do? Were we just to listen to the manipulation of misfortune?

Today, my wife's labor pains became even more obvious. Her stomach was in constant throes of pain, as if a venomous snake were biting her intestines. She tossed and turned on the bed, moaning and wailing. Hearing these sounds, my tears streamed down.

"Ah, this is the struggle of life!" I said to myself.

My wife gradually became exhausted. Thirsty, hungry, she wanted to eat something sour. So I gave her a piece of pineapple (it was canned, a gift from a friend). My wife took it, bit into it twice, and immediately spat it out. The thing seemed to have rotted. I thought: it must be old stock, the friend bought it cheaply.

"Then, have some congee." My wife nodded.

However, she simply couldn't eat it. In the past, we were people who could restrain ourselves and eat a lot. How could there be a reason to not happily eat something when we had it?

"This is the nature of childbirth!" I said to my wife. My wife nodded weakly in pain.

After a lull of less than half an hour, my wife suddenly cried out again. Turning over, her face was pale. That kind of embarrassing and pale countenance made me suspect that I was standing before a critically ill patient. At this moment, the terror and cruelty of death, the pain and bleakness of death, suddenly penetrated my heart again.

Alas, what to do? The hope of hiring a midwife was gone, I was an "outsider" myself, and Zhang next door had gone to the countryside. Relatives were far away from here…

Suddenly, my wife's frantic cry was even more shrill than before. Her forehead was beaded with sweat, her hands pressing on the bed board, a burst of powerless moans, followed by a burst of blood, from there, bathed in purplish-red blood, an innocent baby appeared.

He cried loudly, his voice already containing a kind of worldly suffering.

In this way, my wife luckily escaped the "firing line," but from now on, another burden has been added to our lives!

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talks

Thoughts on "World Animal Day"

— Fang Yin

According to reports, the China Animal Protection Association has obtained the approval of the Executive Yuan to designate October 4th as "World Animal Day," ordering the Ministry of the Interior to instruct governments at all levels to issue notices, exempting slaughter for one day on that day.

And now, this holiday has actually arrived. Whether "military and civilian personnel at all levels" have complied with the order not to eat meat, we naturally cannot know. However, even if everyone does not kill today, I think that once today is over, the animals trapped in cages will definitely not escape their fate of being slaughtered. I remember that it was customary to buy carp to release on "Kitchen God Day." I think this is more straightforward than exempting slaughter for one day (although the former has a purpose). In fact, they arrive at the same destination by different routes: neither can save the lives of the animals.

In the past, there were stories of "long-lived sheep," where people "could not bear to eat their meat upon hearing their cries," but once they turned their backs, they could even "eat human flesh" without any qualms. Therefore, since ancient times, the act of people killing people has continued endlessly, and those who are killed are mostly the weak, like "long-lived sheep." Eleven or twelve years ago, a massacre was staged in Europe. One year after that, many bullies are sharpening their knives in a hurry.

Preachers always attribute people's lives to heaven. Last year's drought and this year's flood are all natural disasters. Therefore, some people say that the lower realm has offended the heavens, so slaughter must be banned and good deeds must be done. As a result, disaster victims are still displaced, die, and wander... However, "benevolent" people still hide in foreign-style houses, and not a grain of rice is given in alms. Moreover, some people will take the opportunity to make a fortune! What is this thing after all: is it benevolence, or is it compassion? ...

Today is a day of exempting slaughter, but what about tomorrow? Are people willing to lay down their butcher knives? — Although I don't worry for the animals, I worry for humanity!

Old Residence

— Tang Wen

I visited a friend but didn't find him at home, so I went to visit my former landlord.

It was in the winter three years ago. After recovering from a serious illness, the doctor instructed me to rest for some time before working. Through a friend's introduction, I rented a corner of a small building here for the lowest rent. The small building faced a park. Every morning, I took a book I loved to read or a newspaper and found a quiet place in the park to read, quietly passing the lonely morning. The landlord was a widower in middle age, with a nine-year-old child studying in elementary school. He himself worked in a bank. When I moved in, it was difficult for us to meet except on Sundays. I got up early, getting up at six o'clock every day, ate a snack, and went to the park across the street, so I often met the newspaper deliveryman's bicycle at the door. I also went to bed early at night. His return time was uncertain. Even if he returned at five o'clock, knowing that I had the habit of going to bed early, only I would go downstairs to meet him. He would never come upstairs, and at that time, the status between guest and host was still maintained. We always had aimless small talk. He was a Catholic. On Sunday mornings, he took his children to church for worship. In the afternoon, we had the opportunity to sit and talk. But after that winter, he lost his job, saying that the bank was laying off employees. That day, he seemed very excited. He came upstairs to my room, took my hand and said: From now on, I will return to my free body! After a few months of cohabitation, we still had not spoken frankly about our own affairs. Although his attitude seemed so sincere that day, I might have thought that he had lost his job a long time ago and said such negative words. I encouraged him like an ordinary friend at the time. He shook his head and held my hand tighter and said:

"My relationship with that bank is very superficial, but my father saved the bank from a crisis when he was alive. After my father died, they gave me a position at will, and they were so generous because there was still a little unfinished business of my father's that needed me to take responsibility for. Then my dismissal was expected a long time ago, but it was just a matter of time. This world completely takes money as the source of power! If it weren't for my father's unfinished responsibility

Page 18

I wouldn't want to float and sink in this place of fame and profit."

From this conversation onwards, our friendship progressed a step further. He had some assets. His current responsibility was to educate his only son. When his wife was dying, she instructed him to remarry her younger sister and treat her flesh and blood well, but he firmly refused to remarry. After that, the pain of his life experience was revealed in the usual conversations. He said that now that he has this free body, he wants to read some books well and learn music to complete his twilight years. Of course, a middle-aged person should not be so negative, but because I sympathize with him, I can no longer say some irrelevant words of encouragement like an ordinary friend.

We lived together for half a year. For the sake of life, I still floated and sank in this place of fame and profit with my weak body. Once I had a job, I was busy running around, and it was rare to have a holiday to wander around my old residence for a day. It has been a few months since I last saw him.

Walking closer to the small building, a melodious piano sound came from the front. I saw the corner of the small building where I had lived for half a year, with green curtains fluttering. A bunch of carnations stretched out their flowers on the window sill. The inner walls also seemed to have been renovated. Listening to the piano sound, it was coming from the building. Although I don't understand what music is being played, the bright piano sound tells me that the musician must be in a happy mood. Perhaps my old friend is playing a piece of music after waking up from a nap, and it is Sunday today, so his son must be waiting by his side. Thinking of this, I felt that my friend was still happy, and I couldn't help but speed up my pace. I pressed the doorbell on the familiar steps, hoping that his son would jump out like a bird, take my hand, and shout "Dad" while running upstairs. But the door was opened by an unfamiliar old woman. I said I wanted to see her master. The old woman replied that her master was in Mogan Mountain and had not returned, and the two young ladies were in Shanghai. I asked about their surname. It turned out that my old friend and his son had gone to another place two months ago, and this small building had changed owners. I wanted to know more details, but the old woman shook her head and closed the door.

Standing in front of the door, feeling lost, I heard the piano sound playing melodiously again inside.

To Changsha

— Ai Tu

(The Changsha mentioned here is not the resounding Changsha in Hunan, but a relatively famous Changsha Island near the sea in our Guangdong.)

Before taking a ferry from Guangzhou to Sanbu to Changsha, I spent a night on the sea. In autumn, the sea at night is very beautiful. The calm river water flows gently, completely unlike the turbulent sea, which flashes dangerous and charming silvery-white waves. However, the river surface at night here also has many intoxicating shadows, as if it has reached a poetic and alluring realm. Although I can't see the singing and dancing girls wearing enchanting clothes like in the city, I can hear the rustling wind in the calm countryside plains. This faint and heart-soaking wind has a certain rhythm. Who says it's not charming! On the river surface on such a silent night, hearing it is like hearing the song of poetry! Therefore, I always forget the time to sleep, pacing quietly on the deck, my eyes looking at a distant and hazy wilderness. Wilderness! It was blown by the wind swept over from the South China Sea, like countless girls swaying and twisting their waists. Even when I looked up at the sky, the clear sky was covered with countless stars. Who says the river at night is not beautiful! So, my heart unknowingly melted into the beautiful rural travel. Yes, in Shanghai, I have never had such happiness, never had such a feeling.

When I had heard enough of the wind howling and the rushing river water flowing, and I was tired and it was time to go to sleep, I hid in the cabin, dreaming and praying for tomorrow morning. Tomorrow I will be in Changsha! That is a sandbar surrounded by rivers! There should be many beautiful scenery there for me to enjoy! The young wanderer thought so.

When I woke up the next day, the sun hadn't climbed up earlier than me. I ran to the deck again, breathing the light and fresh air, and looking at the quiet scenery on both sides of the river. When the boat passed Gongyi, the sun was just climbing out, and the entire earth was covered with bright red and gorgeous clothes. The green mountain peaks and the green forests were all flashing with red clouds! This lovely morning is not something I could enjoy when I was wandering in Shanghai.

When I arrived in Changsha, I could see a new place, three ports - Xinchang, Dihai and Changsha - standing side by side next to the sea. The buildings are all like Guangzhou, neat and beautiful. Yes, this is also a place built with the blood and sweat of overseas Chinese. On the one hand, Changsha Island, in addition to the distant and vast plains and villages in the bamboo forests, is the long street market. This place is not very strange. I traveled here in earlier years. Now, I can call it revisiting an old place. Yes, I love this place very much, because this big sandbar is very interesting. If a few friends use a small boat to circle the entire island for a week at dusk, it will only take four or five hours, but we can see many natural and unadorned scenery, completely unlike the West Lake, which is dyed with the colors of the capitalist market, and even more unlike the hypocrisy of the prosperous and dead big city! If you take a walk in the criss-crossing fields, the charming posture of the green rice fields is all simple, and although the scenery of this place is not bright, basically, if it is decorated a little, I always believe that it is a very famous sandbar park. (But, then I won't be happy to come and visit!)

Isn't that right? I have a habit and a hobby. I love to eat fresh rapeseed more than anything else. This is a place famous for producing fruit.

When I arrived at Changsha Pier, I carried my simple luggage around the streets. At the end of the streets is Zhongshan Park, which is full of lotus leaves in the ponds. Yes, that is the school where I am going to stay. When our friends came out to pick me up, I saw more than 300 children, beautiful girls, all looking at me with cheerful and kind eyes. So, I unknowingly mixed with the naughty and innocent children. Everything was as lovely as the morning sun. When the children all left, I leaned on the railings of the third floor to look at the public countries in front, the distant and curved river water, the flat buildings, and breathed the fresh air. So, everything dispelled the depression in my heart.

The Whole Family is in the Autumn Wind

— Jiang Mi

Eastern Travel Notes

— Liu Bing

Maybe it's just my personal bias, but after coming to Tokyo, everything makes me feel very fresh. Friend, because you are also curious, I will tell you what I have seen and heard.

The first thing that made me feel fresh after coming to Tokyo was the Japanese people's clothing. Of course, in Shanghai, you often see Japanese people's clothes, but in Shanghai, young girls have already worn Western clothes. It may be very rare to see a young girl wearing Eastern clothes, so this makes me feel fresh. When I arrived, it was the time of late summer and early autumn. They all put bright, large floral patterns on their bodies, with two sleeves dragging down to their knees, and their hair separated into two halves at the back. Walking, they are lively and quiet. When we look at them from behind, we will think of a beautiful butterfly. I once went to a dance hall with a friend. There, I saw dancers wearing brightly colored "kimonos." Their sleeves were even longer and bigger. When they danced, their sleeves fluttered in the wind, which was really beautiful.

In the eyes of us foreigners, the clothing of Japanese women seems to be roughly the same. In fact, its changes are no less than the cheongsam of our country's women. Not only does the style change from time to time, but the patterns also change with the seasons. Therefore, whenever the season is about to change, major companies display dozens of new spring or autumn "visiting clothes" from 1935 on a certain floor. The styles and patterns are very gorgeous. The so-called "visiting clothes" are the most important and precious clothes in "kimono," which are worn when going out or visiting friends. They are very expensive, some costing several hundred yen a day. Just a visiting belt also costs more than thirty yen. The pattern styles of these "visiting clothes" are all designed by designers in "kimono shops." Every change in pattern style, even if it is so subtle that we cannot see it, Japanese women know whether it is a popular pattern at a glance. However, these are naturally limited to idle wives and young ladies. As for those working women, such as female ticket sellers and maids, they have no time to pay attention to these.

Men's clothing is relatively simple. In addition to wearing "kimonos," many people already wear "suits" for convenience at work. However, their suits are also very casual. It doesn't matter if they are wider or narrower, and the style is even less of a concern for which year. Even if you wear the style of 1925, you are far from the people of 1935. Unlike our country's personnel departments, after people, only decorations must be the first to grab. Before 1935 has arrived, the style of 1936 will be out of date.

Speaking of the clothing of Japanese students, it is even more worth noting. Whether in elementary, middle, or university, male and female students must wear student uniforms. At the same time, they absolutely do not pay attention to it, and they are even proud of wearing old and worn student uniforms. Some students use their hats to wipe tables and benches, so that the hats are worn to a shiny mirror surface, which is enough to show their qualifications. And the students of the Imperial University also hang a towel on their garter, hanging outside. Walking, swaying, it simply makes you laugh, but they take this as "spirited," so our Chinese students studying in Japan, after a long time, also learn the appearance of Japanese students, hiding their good suits and wearing student uniforms all day long.

There are many styles of female students' clothing, but most wear skirts and shirts. They value skirts very much. Wearing skirts means being polite. Their skirts are all added on the outside, bloated and unbearable. Although we laugh when we see it, they think that this is the polite behavior of intellectuals.

The clothing of Chinese students studying in Japan, if they come from the country for the first time, will not change for a while, and many still wear beautiful suits. Therefore, everyone says, "East Asian students are the most fashionable." In fact, this means that they are new to Tokyo and are not yet qualified to wear student uniforms. After a year or half a year, they will naturally change. However, it is more difficult for women to change. No matter how many years they live in Tokyo, they always like to wear cheongsams, which is probably because they are more comfortable and convenient.

Miscellaneous Thoughts

— Yang Zhongshuo

I have become more and more lonely recently. I have become quite interested in the Buddhist teachings of Zen Buddhism, but I am still very young and unwilling to let my life be tainted with negativity. This self-reflection is a skill that I have only recently developed.

Thinking of my depravity, I inevitably tend to be on the road to degeneration, so I cheer up my cold heart again, and pay attention to people, things, and learning. However, a more serious life provokes the hatred of friends. A lonely personality is not a talent, but a result of the environment.

The change of seasons has given me some stimulation. The rustling autumn wind blows my disheveled hair, and it has also made me feel lonely and desolate. I have also expressed sympathetic pity for those withered and yellow fallen leaves. A small boat on the river has also aroused a lot of poetic and pictorial ideas, but after all, I am not a painter with a skillful hand and have not painted this natural picture on paper. I am also not a poet and have not chanted this beautiful scenery into a clear and easy-to-read poem. All my experiences are expressed between the lines. I have also cursed my own shallowness.

It is autumn. The river water is no longer as turbid as in summer, but facing the turbulent waves, I seem to have gained this enlightenment: life should be like the tide, advancing bravely and destroying all thorns and fences!

Many people come here from distant places in this season of high autumn, clear sky, gentle breeze and warm sunshine. Perhaps the vast river arouses their infinite interest, or perhaps the high tower standing on the bank of the river gives them a lot of thoughts of nostalgia. They come in batches and go in batches.

The maple leaves on the mountain are already red, swaying in the wind like a shy girl dancing. I remember that Suiyuan once had these two lines of poetry about maple trees: "Sometimes falling at will on the grass, there is no such pitiful red in the flowers." It is really a vivid portrayal.

Movies

Heavenly Love's Dubbing Music Orientalized

In the past, many domestic films were produced with music, but most of them were taken from Western music. Occasionally, some Chinese music was produced, but this so-called Chinese music was just a very common Cantonese tune. As for whether the mixed music can help the performance effect of the play, it is difficult to say. Lianfeng took this dubbing of "Heavenly Love" very seriously. Special talents were hired to continue working day and night, striving to integrate the music with the film to achieve a mixed aesthetic effect. Moreover, the music used is extremely avoided from phonograph record-like rotten tunes. The score should be specially composed for this play, to make it orientalized. Such creation is worthy of attention.

Silver Pen Miscellany

— Wen Er

Not long ago, the Star Film Company laid off 102 junior employees to save expenses. It is said that Mr. Li Pingqian was in charge.

Now, it is rumored that Mr. Li Pingqian will also leave the Star Film Company. The reason? Not detailed.

The news that the Star Film Company has restored the screenwriting department and hired Ouyang Yuqian and Liu Naou as screenwriters has already been revealed in other newspapers.

Let's not mention this here. Let's say that according to the news we heard, it is: in addition to the above two, there is also Huang Tianshi. "Soft as cotton and smooth as oil", under the leadership of Liu Huang and others, the future Star productions will mostly be soft works, right?

After Liu Huang and others were honorably appointed as screenwriters of the Star Film Company, Mr. Yao Suifeng was also honorably appointed as a "special screenwriter" of the Star Film Company. It is said that Mr. Yao originally planned to officially enter the Star Film Company, but it did not work out for other reasons.

The boring things like female stars unveiling for others are becoming less and less now.

Zhang Wen, a newcomer from Yi Hua, played a boat girl in "At the Beginning of Man" (this is what I learned from the publicity draft), and a nurse in "The Tempest". Probably to promote newcomers, Yi Hua also specifically issued a "Newcomer Zhang Wen" publicity draft.

What I saw was a fleeting glimpse in "At the Beginning of Man", and I didn't even see her face clearly. In "The Tempest", she had more scenes than in "At the Beginning of Man". This time, people can see her face clearly (but if it weren't for the instructions in the manual, I'm afraid I still wouldn't be able to see it)?

Therefore, I understand the meaning of the four words "promote newcomers" and the function of the instruction manual.

African War Premieres

At this critical moment of the treacherous Italian-Abyssinian situation, "African War" is something that we should pay great attention to. This film is a famous adventure novel by British literary master Edgar Wallace, which describes all kinds of inevitable human tragedies. However, the plot is very tragic and lingering, and the natural background is great and beautiful. The protagonist is the black genius superstar Paul Robeson (Paul Robeson will star in "The Emperor Jones", that is, "The Emperor Jones"). A contribution from the authoritative American Lianmei Company in the film industry, now showing in "Nanjing".

Golden City Premieres "The Tempest"

Yi Hua Company's latest masterpiece, directed by Yuan Congmei, starring Yuan Meiyun, Wei Heling, Wang Naidong, Cang Yinqiu, Qin Tong, Liu Zhao, etc., photography by Wu Weiyun, scenery by Fang Feilin, and all-sound singing and dancing dialogue silver film by Gu Zongyi, "The Tempest", will be premiered at the Golden City Theater on the 2nd. The characteristics of this film are not only that the director is good, the photography is good, the scenery is good, the sound is good, and the actors are good, but especially the three major problems of "life", "society" and "era" hinted in the play have bold, accurate and profound positive reviews and sideways irony. It tells you the sins and contradictions of life in the society of the current era, and also tells you how people should struggle and work hard in the society of the current era. Therefore, it can be said that it is a work that deals with the personal problems of the hard-pressed people in the current era. Men and women who are struggling in the current society all need to learn from this play the current way out and the need to improve their lifestyle.
